[维权网：中国大陆在押政治犯、良心犯月度报告（2021年11月30日）第74期（共 1189人）(五）](https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2021/11/2021113074-1189_86.html)
------

<div>
<p><span></span></p><a name='more'></a>&nbsp;<p></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">续上，第五部分：（<span lang="EN-US">M</span>、<span lang="EN-US">N</span>、<span lang="EN-US">O</span>、<span lang="EN-US">P</span>、<span lang="EN-US">Q</span>、<span lang="EN-US">R</span>、<span lang="EN-US">S</span>）</span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 22.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">M.<o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">马宝玲、马春、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">马凤菊、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">马海鹏、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">马海云、马纳普汗（哈萨克）、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">马庆霞、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">马少杰</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">马淑芬、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">马义涛、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">马永菊</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、马玉凤、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">马智武</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">玛乌提•么斯尔汗（哈萨克）、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">麦尔丹•赛伊塔洪（维吾尔）、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">买买提江•阿布都拉（维吾尔）、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">买吾拉尼•努尔买买提（维）</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">、</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">曼嘎（藏）、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">毛德君</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">米久平、米玛顿珠（藏）、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">明经国、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">孟凡军、孟凯、孟丽春、孟庆素、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">孟素英</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、孟宪强、孟祥岐、孟晓东、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">莫伟秋、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">牟永霞</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">穆塔力浦•伊明（维吾尔）、木拉提别克．吾麻尔（哈）、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">马宝玲<span lang="EN-US">: </span></span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">江苏省连云港市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日，连云港市海州区公安分局抓捕了法轮功学员刘玉萍、邵世玲、那仁志、熊成霞、周翠萍、马宝玲、高建君、王艾芝、汪宝玉、小周女士、乔老太等十一人。所有人家中都被非法抄了家，警察劫走家中的电脑、手机、光盘、<span lang="EN-US">U</span>盘、电器、钱财、书籍等私人物品。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日，马宝玲被开庭，被判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">马春：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1973</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日出生，江苏省徐州市睢宁县人，睢宁县睢城镇南关小区和平村<span lang="EN-US">11</span>号公民，江苏金和律师事务所（睢宁）执业律师，蒙冤维权律师，中国在押维权人士。自幼被亲生父母遗弃，后被养父母收养，性情温和良善；曾因酷喜读书，尤爱律师职业，随于<span lang="EN-US">2002</span>年考取司法资格证书，实习后开始成为一名克己敬业的执业律师；曾因多次尽心尽责做无偿法律援助，帮助当事人维护合法权益，而深得当事人及业界同仁的信任和称赞，曾被人冠以“阿甘律师”的美誉；<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年，曾因代理一起民事案件，被当事人王雪鸿刻意陷害，谎称其与该当事人的债权人一起倾吞自己厂房；其对此据理力争，不断呼吁与维权，后经执行局查证，得知该当事人王雪鸿竟是公认的老赖（即赖账不还者）；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月，曾因江苏省警方成立项目组对睢宁县夏氏兄弟涉黑案立案侦查，而其曾于<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年系本案受害人王雪鸿的法律顾问，随被莫名其妙、蒙冤卷入一起套路贷涉黑案；<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2018</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日，其突然失踪，家属报案无果，直至一周后的<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日，才知其已被徐州市丰县警方带到丰县宾馆，被以涉嫌欺诈为由指定居所监视居住<span lang="EN-US">46</span>天；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年，其被丰县检察院以涉嫌“诈骗罪和非法拘禁罪”予以批捕，指控其曾“伙同夏氏、李巍等人诈骗”，又“非法拘禁王雪鸿，侵吞其远鸿公司食品厂”，故而其行为触犯了政府的有关刑法条例规定；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日，其案在江苏省徐州市丰县法院开庭受理，后因感觉案件复杂，随在庭审六天后匆匆收场；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，再被庭审，最终被徐州市丰县法院一审以“诈骗罪”判刑<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，“非法拘禁罪”判刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，二罪并罚，执行判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>个月，罚金人民币<span lang="EN-US">25</span>万，<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2029</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日；</b>其不服，上诉至徐州市中级法院；据悉，其一直坚称无罪，并曾在一审庭审时，声称其在监视居住期间遭刑讯逼供，疲劳审几乎使他精神几乎崩溃；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日，其与律师会见时又表示，其一直无法通过看守所将写好的辩护材料交给法院及律师；二审正在等待中。目前被羁押于徐州市丰县看守所。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><a name="_Hlk52181848"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">马凤菊：</span></b></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk52181848;"></span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">辽宁省清原县法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日，马凤菊、刘玉英在清原易和小区发放法轮功资料，被清原镇河南派出所警察王东等人抓捕，被关押在抚顺看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日开庭，未当庭宣判。后获悉，马凤菊被判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，刘玉英被判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 106%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">马海鹏：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">陕西咸阳市法轮功学员。研究生毕业。咸阳市<span lang="EN-US">4</span>名法轮功学员</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">张鹏、王钰超、臧金达、马海鹏因为向淳化县民众发放真相资料，于<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月至<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月先后在各自的住所被淳化县公安局警察抓捕抄家。张鹏、王钰超（<span lang="EN-US">26</span>岁左右）<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月底在咸阳市住处被警察绑架，电脑、打印机等设备被抢走。<span lang="EN-US">4</span>位法轮功学员被关押在咸阳淳化县看守所，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月获悉<span lang="EN-US">4</span>人均已被判刑，其中张鹏判刑<span lang="EN-US">9</span>年，王钰超、臧金达、马海鹏约为<span lang="EN-US">5</span>至<span lang="EN-US">9</span>年不等，刑期不详。。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/8/30/2021-8-30.html#zip3"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/8/30/2021-8-30.html#zip3</span></b></a></span><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">马海云：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">女，<span lang="EN-US">1962</span>年生。安徽淮南市田家庵区法轮功学员。原是电子工业部第八研究所（淮南）光缆车间职工。<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月中共迫害法轮功后，马海云因为坚持信仰，多次被非法关押，<span lang="EN-US">2003</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月份，被判刑<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年。<span lang="EN-US">2004</span>年元月份，马海云被非法关押到安徽省女子监狱。她丈夫许渝发也多次遭受迫害，被迫流离失所。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日下午，马海云在免费赠送法轮功资料时，被人恶意举报，遭淮南市国庆路派出所警察抓捕抄家，抢走手机、电脑等私人财物。马海云被刑事拘留，关押在淮南市看守所。家人给她送衣物，被看守所拒绝。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日在淮南市田家庵区法院被开庭，后悉被非法判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">马纳普汗（哈萨克）：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">新疆阿尔泰地区哈萨克族居民，哈萨克族良心犯、人权捍卫者。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月，因其获得一本从哈萨克斯坦国带回的《古兰经》，所以被当地公安局将其一家三口悉数抓走，并被指控“持有非法宗教出版物”。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月，其“持古兰经案”被当地法院开庭审理，一家三口分别被以“持有非法宗教出版物罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年。开庭前，其要求聘请律师遭拒。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">马庆霞：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">天津市法轮功学员。女，<span lang="EN-US">1979</span>年生，家住天津市武清区黄庄乡<span lang="EN-US">6</span>合庄村。<span lang="EN-US">2006</span>年，马庆霞开始修炼法轮功。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日晚上<span lang="EN-US">7</span>点多钟，马庆霞家来了<span lang="EN-US">7</span>、<span lang="EN-US">8</span>个警察，抄家，抄走大法书籍、两台计算机、真相币、墙上的壁画和<span lang="EN-US">1</span>万多元钱等私人物品，并让马庆霞签字，马庆霞没有配合警察的要求，没有签字。警察将马庆霞抓捕到黄庄派出所，第<span lang="EN-US">2</span>天，转到刑警队关押。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日得知，被在看守所的马庆霞遭批捕。现得知，马庆霞被武清区法院被判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日，被劫入天津女子监狱，被关押在<span lang="EN-US">9</span>监区。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 39.95pt; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">马少杰：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">女士，<span lang="EN-US">1950</span>年代生人，山东临清国棉厂法轮功学员。一九九九年七月中共迫害法轮功后，马少杰多次被中共绑架、非法关押。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日，马少杰发放真相资料，被临清市公安局青年派出所警察抓捕，当日晚七点多被放回家。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日早晨，马少杰又被临清市“六一零”、临清市公安局国保大队从家中绑架，关押聊城地区看守所。后被刑事拘留、批捕、起诉。后获悉判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>个月。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年中国新年前，马少杰女士被转入山东省女子监狱迫害。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">马淑芬：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">天津市河北区法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">1944</span>年生，退休教师，<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月，被检察院、法院构陷，准备对她判刑。法院以岁数大可以从轻处理，但是不放弃炼法轮功，就严判为条件，企图让马淑芬放弃修炼法轮功，马淑芬拒绝。在<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月中旬，马淑芬被判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。在天津女子监狱服刑。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">马义涛：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">黑龙江省北安市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日夜晚，马义涛等三名法轮功学员开车到五大连池市发放法轮功真相资料。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日凌晨，他们被跟踪的警察抓捕，同时被抓捕的法轮功学员还有李学良、盛春霞。随后警察驱车到北安市城区马义涛的家抄家，抢劫走几本大法著作和真相资料，并抓捕了马义涛的妻子马英杰。）<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，马义涛等四人被黑龙江省亚布力林区法院判刑。马义涛被判<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年，李学良<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，马英杰<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，盛春霞判三年缓四年，已回家。马义涛、李学良不服法院非法判决，提出上诉。马义涛刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">马永菊：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">女，贵州省六盘水市钟山区汪家寨镇法轮功学员。在中共对法轮功的迫害中，马永菊曾五次被抓捕、关押，其中两次被劳教，屡遭酷刑。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月下旬被朝阳派出所警察抓捕到大丫口拘留所关押、构陷；马永菊<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日被六盘水市钟山区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年、罚金一万元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 351.75pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">马玉凤：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">江苏省镇江市润州区维权人士。因为在<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年清明时，到北京福田公墓祭奠杨佳，在“十一”维稳时，被公安以“涉嫌寻衅滋事罪”指定监视居住。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年的最后一天，马玉凤直接由指定监视居住转为批捕。目前无具体信息。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">马智武：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">原是宁夏银川铁路分局安全监察室的司机，<span lang="EN-US">1971</span>年生。<span lang="EN-US">1998</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月开始修炼法轮大法。<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月中共迫害法轮功后，马智武去北京为法轮功上访，被劳教<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，遭受生不如死的折磨，他绝食反迫害，却被中共的判刑<span lang="EN-US">6</span>年。<span lang="EN-US">2010</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日，马智武再次被抓捕，判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年半。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月初，马智武回固原市老家找活干。<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日，在宁夏公安厅有关人员、固原市原州区国保大队冯队长、教导员杨富春的操控下，马智武在老家固原市泾源县被抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日，宁夏固原市中级法院法官到固原市看守所向马智武宣读了该院<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日签署的所谓《刑事判决书》：马智武被固原市中级法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">14</span>年，其中「利用邪教组织破坏法律实施罪」判<span lang="EN-US">13</span>年，「煽动颠覆国家政权罪」判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年，合并执行<span lang="EN-US">14</span>年，罚款<span lang="EN-US">3</span>万元。其不服上诉；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月，经宁夏回族自治区高级法院不公开二审裁决，依然维持原判，刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2034</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2021/09/14.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2021/09/14.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">玛乌提•么斯尔汗（哈萨克）：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">他与</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">纳杂尔﹒叶尔江、哈纳提别克﹒萨布尔别克、阿尔恒﹒巴杂尔别克、乌木别提﹒卡斯木、哈伊拉提别克﹒木合塔尔汗、沙部旦﹒沙伊合、耶尔肯别克﹒达列力、肯杰别克﹒达列力都是新疆伊利市哈萨克自治州阿尔泰市巴里巴盖乡人，哈萨克族，穆斯林。其中，纳杂尔﹒叶尔江<span lang="EN-US">26</span>岁，哈纳提别克﹒萨布尔别克<span lang="EN-US">26</span>岁，阿尔恒﹒巴杂尔别克<span lang="EN-US">27</span>岁，乌木别提﹒卡斯木<span lang="EN-US">31</span>岁，哈伊拉提别克﹒木合塔尔汗<span lang="EN-US">37</span>岁，沙部旦﹒沙伊合约<span lang="EN-US">30</span>岁，耶尔肯别克﹒达列力<span lang="EN-US">30</span>岁，肯杰别克﹒达列力<span lang="EN-US">27</span>岁，玛乌提﹒么斯尔汗约<span lang="EN-US">30</span>岁。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">-8</span>月，因他们分别在私下里进行了穆斯林传统常规祷告仪式，而被中共新疆伊犁市哈萨克自治州阿尔泰当局知晓后拘捕，遂很快被阿尔泰市地方法院以“非法从事宗教活动”和“从事宗教极端活动”为由分别判处<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">-6</span>年不等刑期。目前各人具体判刑不详，刑至日期不详，服刑监狱不详，服刑状况及健康程度等不详。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">麦尔丹•赛伊塔洪（维吾尔）：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">新疆维吾尔自治区伊犁哈萨克族自治州伊宁县人，因笃信伊斯兰教，同时又经常收留流落街头的儿童，宣传和教育他们学做好人、遵守宗教道德，从而碰触到当局的敏感神经；又因中共长期以来对维吾尔人的宗教信仰采取高压控制政策（中共当局相关法规规定，凡私自进行宗教信仰教育属违法行为，凡私自指导、主持伊斯兰教教育属从事“非法”宗教活动），不仅对进出清真寺的人员实施全面监控，而且对<span lang="EN-US">18</span>岁以下维吾尔青少年、维吾尔共产党员进寺礼拜更是予以极力限制，尤其是明令禁止跨村礼拜，限制朝觐，严禁穿“伊斯兰”服饰，禁止学生及公务员按宗教教义习俗封斋等，故而在<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月—<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月的新疆地区宗教活动大抓捕行动中，在伊犁哈萨克族自治州伊宁县和尼勒克县竟抓捕了<span lang="EN-US">12</span>名伊斯兰教宣传者；在此高压管控下，<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日<span lang="EN-US">,</span>其亦被伊宁市警方以涉嫌“分裂国家罪”刑拘，并被指控有向青少年灌输“非法”宗教的行为，属从事以“分裂主义”为目的的非法宗教活动，是“分裂分子”，后被以同罪名正式逮捕；<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日被新疆维吾尔自治区伊犁中级法院以“分裂国家罪”秘密判处无期徒刑；其代理律师被政府指定。目前在新疆维吾尔自治区伊犁哈萨克族自治州伊宁县监狱服刑。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">买买提江•阿布都拉（维吾尔）</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">：<span lang="EN-US">1977</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日出生，新疆维吾尔自治区克拉玛依人，原中央人民广播电台维语部播音员、记者、编辑，业余担任维语彩丽肯（清风）网（<span lang="EN-US">salkin.cn</span>）主持人，独立中文笔会荣誉会员，中国在押政治犯、良心犯。<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年因广东韶关<span lang="EN-US">6</span>•<span lang="EN-US">26</span>事件后接受境外记者采访，把世界维吾尔大会发言人的示威号召等一些汉语敏感文章翻译成维语，发表在中国境内维语网站彩丽肯网（<span lang="EN-US">salkin.cn</span>），有协助煽动之后乌鲁木齐<span lang="EN-US">7</span>•<span lang="EN-US">5</span>事件的嫌疑，遂于<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月被警方逮捕；<span lang="EN-US">2010</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日，买买提江•阿布都拉被新疆乌鲁木齐市中级人民法院以“分裂国家、泄露国家秘密和组织非法示威罪”判处无期徒刑。目前在新疆维吾尔自治区伊犁哈萨克自治州塔城的乌苏监狱服刑。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">买吾拉尼•努尔买买提</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">：新疆维吾尔自治区博尔塔拉蒙古自治州博乐市人，原新疆中国电信员工，互联网技术个体工商户，博乐市易信通信设施安装有限公司创办人，中国在押政治犯。早期曾为新疆中国电信公司<span lang="EN-US">1</span>职员，后离职开创属于自己的小本生意，主要负责互联网相关技术的运营；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月，曾在新疆博乐市成立和注册“博乐市易信通信设施安装有限公司”，收益较丰；<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月，随着中共政府对新疆地区各少数民族（尤以维吾尔族、哈萨克斯坦族、回族等居多）要求民族独立自治、要求信仰自由等要求的极端管控和打击，新疆出现大规模维吾尔族及其他少数民族穆斯林被关进“再教育营”现象，在此氛围下，其亦被博尔塔拉蒙古自治州博乐市警方莫名抓捕，自此失踪；后经其家人长期搜寻，知其先被博乐市公安局送至<span lang="EN-US">1</span>个“再教育营”关押，但因表现不佳，拒不配合洗脑教育，又被以涉嫌“分裂国家”罪由予以逮捕；<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月，被博乐市地方法院<span lang="EN-US">1</span>审以“分裂国家政权罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">9</span>年；其不服上诉；后经博尔塔拉蒙古自治州中级法院<span lang="EN-US">2</span>审裁决：驳回上诉，维持原判；据悉，<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日已被移交到监狱服刑；中国政府曾就其被抓判刑向联合国工作小组提供信息称，其之前无业，其家人表示愤慨；刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月。目前在新疆石河子市北野监狱（石河子市北野镇 邮政编码<span lang="EN-US">: 832028</span>）服刑。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">曼嘎：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">女，四川省甘孜藏族羌族自治区州阿坝县麦尔玛乡藏人，父亲名叫次培，母亲叫白玛吉。麦尔玛乡在过去一年中曾发生多起独自游街抗议中共暴政的活动。<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年中共当局在麦尔玛乡境内强迫每户藏人家庭悬挂中共五星红旗，当时曼嘎不但拒绝这一无理要求，并与官方人员争辩，结果被非法关押<span lang="EN-US">8</span>个多月，其间遭受了折磨虐待。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日中午<span lang="EN-US">12</span>点左右，曼嘎在麦尔玛乡一处街道上独自开展了示威活动，当时曼嘎双手举着达赖喇嘛尊者的法像，并呼喊出口号，中共公安随即赶到现场将她拘捕。后音信全无。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">毛德君：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">女，<span lang="EN-US">1954</span>年生，山东莒南县，法轮功学员，东北某中学退休物理教师。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日，莒南县警察抓捕了法轮功学员毛德君。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，在北京维权律师做出无罪辩护情况下，山东省临沂市临沭县法院法官吴淑芳，对莒南县法轮功学员毛德君女士，枉法判决<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 351.75pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">米久平：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">深圳佳士工人。因要求组建独立工会，<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日被深圳警方以寻衅滋事罪刑事拘留，同时被刑事拘留的有<span lang="EN-US">14</span>名工人。关押在深圳龙岗区看守所。已关押两年多，未有案件进展信息。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">米玛顿珠（藏）：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">1973</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">年出生，西藏自治区日喀则定日县人，藏名<span lang="EN-US">Migmar Dhondup</span>，社会工作者，中国在押政治犯。曾于<span lang="EN-US">1990</span>年代中期在南印度某学院研读商务课程，后返回西藏，致力于为百姓谋福利，在山南和拉萨地区，与当地农民和牧民一起努力改善卫生条件，规划社会发展计划，并呼吁西方人支持和参与这些计划；<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月，因在拉萨市<span lang="EN-US">3</span>•<span lang="EN-US">14</span>事件中参与和平抗议活动而被当局逮捕，同年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日，又以“接受西藏流亡政府指派，在拉萨建立地下情报网络，大量复制并散发具有煽动分裂国家内容的光盘和煽动‘举行西藏人民大起义运动’的传单，以及给境外收集涉及国家安全和利益的情报”等为由，被拉萨市中级法院以“间谍罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">14</span>年，剥夺政治权利<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年。 目前在西藏自治区拉萨市曲水监狱服刑。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 351.75pt;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">明经国：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">江西赣州南康乡<span lang="EN-US">6</span>旬农民明经国反强拆锄杀官员案。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日上午，该乡人大主席卓宇和村干部多人再次来到村民明经国家，强拆明经国祖屋，遭反抗。卓宇被明经国用镰铲击伤，因伤势过重送医后死亡。<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日上午，明经国被捕，后被刑事拘留，<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日开庭审理，开庭未判。</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">江西反强拆明经国“锄死”乡干部案<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日宣判，明经国被赣州中院以故意杀人罪一审判处死刑，缓期<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年执行，剥夺政治权利终身。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">孟凡军：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">于健莉一家七人法轮功案受害人之一。吉林长春市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，四平市公安局、梨树县公安局出动几百警力，包括四平市公安局国保大队、梨树县公安局国保大队、巡警、交警、梨树县辖区内各派出所警察，还调动所辖社区的部份人员，并在长春市当地警察的配合下，在长春市开始了对法轮功学员及其家属的绑架，并到在省内其它地区居住的学员及亲属家中进行绑架。于健莉一家七人在各自的家被公安警察绑架。包括：于健莉、母亲付贵华、丈夫王东吉、公公王克民、婆婆王凤芝、妹夫孟祥岐，及孟祥岐的父亲孟凡军。后一家七人均被判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年至<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年半，其中付贵华和孟祥岐被非法判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年半，其余<span lang="EN-US">5</span>人为<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">孟凯：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">1970</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年代出生，湖北省人，长沙市某公司法务工作者，自由信仰追求者，法轮功修炼者，中国在押良心犯。早期曾就读于武汉华中农业大学法律系，毕业后成为一名执业律师，并曾参加研究生考试；<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年起，中共开始迫害法轮功，因其信仰和练习法轮功，并曾将<span lang="EN-US">2000</span>张法轮功宣传数据从湖南长沙带到岳阳进行宣传，随被“<span lang="EN-US">601</span>”发监管办公室监控人员举报、刑拘，后被湖南省岳阳市法院枉判<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年；获释后，因其全家搬到长沙市，其随家人一同亦迁至长沙市居住；<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">2019</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月，其开始在一家公司做法务工作，并因平日工作敬业，积极为公司解决了许多搁置已久、悬而未决的事项，从而获得公司法务部总管及同事们的普遍赞扬；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，其在前往外地帮公司打官司的途中，突遭湖南省浏阳市警方抓捕，后得知亦有另<span lang="EN-US">20</span>余名法轮功信仰者（含多名博士生、高干、律师等各类人士）同期均被湖南省长沙市当局以涉嫌“邪教罪”刑拘；次日，其旋即又被以同罪名转正式逮捕，且被关押在长沙市第一看守所；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日，其家属及代理律师知其已被秘密判刑，刑期不清；据悉，因其拒绝认罪，负责其案的警方曾称，“这个态度要判他<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年”；其代理律师请求与其会见，遭拒，其家属到监狱要求探视，亦遭拒绝。目前被羁押于长沙监狱进行“洗脑式”培训，之后将被转至何监狱服刑，暂且不明。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">孟丽春</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">：哈尔滨市依兰县法轮功学员。女，原哈尔滨市依兰县珠山中学教师。一九九九年七月二十日，中共开始迫害法轮功，孟丽春被中共绑架、关押，曾被非法劳教三年。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，孟丽春在双鸭山市集贤县租住房中，被依兰县公安局警察秘密跟踪、抓捕，被关押在哈尔滨市第二看守所迫害。中共不法人员一年半时间没让家人探视孟丽春。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月孟丽春家人获悉，她被秘密判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，关押到黑龙江省女子监狱迫害。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">孟庆素：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">四川省成都市人，成都市双流区西航港莲花小区居民，法轮功信仰者、良心犯。因信仰、宣传法轮功，<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日被成都市公安局天府新区分局警方非法绑架，并于<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日在成都市双流区法院非法开庭。在庭上，尽管其拒绝认罪，且其辩护律师认为该案所列证据不足以作为定罪依据，被告人的行为不构成犯罪，但最终仍被该法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">孟素英：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">黑龙江省齐齐哈尔市法轮功学员。孙广利、孟素英夫妇，黑龙江省齐齐哈尔市碾子山区人，暂住辽宁省沈阳市。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日晚<span lang="EN-US">7</span>点多孙广利、孟素英夫妇，在沈阳市辽中区<span lang="EN-US">6</span>间房镇的<span lang="EN-US">1</span>个村子里发了几张告诉世人如何躲避瘟疫的方法，被人诬告，<span lang="EN-US">6</span>间房派出所的警察将<span lang="EN-US">2</span>人抓捕到当地派出所进行关押。 由于那时中国疫情严重，看守所不接收，次日晚<span lang="EN-US">7</span>点多将<span lang="EN-US">2</span>人放回家中。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日晚<span lang="EN-US">7</span>点左右，东街派出所的<span lang="EN-US">5</span>、<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个警察又到家中将夫妻<span lang="EN-US">2</span>人强行抓捕到东街派出所。<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日晚，丈夫孙广利被关押到沈阳第二看守所，妻子孟素英被关押到沈阳第一看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日傍晚，他们的家人接到法院通知：孙广利、孟素英夫妇判决已下来，最终两人均被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">孟宪强：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">山东潍坊市昌乐县法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日下午，昌乐县红河镇法轮功学员孟宪强被红河镇派出所警察非法抄家并绑架。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日被山东青州法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年<span lang="EN-US">.</span>刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5 </span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">孟祥岐：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">于健莉一家七人法轮功案受害人之一。吉林长春市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，四平市公安局、梨树县公安局出动几百警力，包括四平市公安局国保大队、梨树县公安局国保大队、巡警、交警、梨树县辖区内各派出所警察，还调动所辖社区的部份人员，并在长春市当地警察的配合下，在长春市开始了对法轮功学员及其家属的绑架，并到在省内其它地区居住的学员及亲属家中进行绑架。于健莉一家七人在各自的家被公安警察绑架。包括：于健莉、母亲付贵华、丈夫王东吉、公公王克民、婆婆王凤芝、妹夫孟祥岐，及孟祥岐的父亲孟凡军。后一家七人均被判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年至<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年半，其中付贵华和孟祥岐被非法判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年半，其余<span lang="EN-US">5</span>人为<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">孟晓东：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">（身份证名字孟跟东<span lang="EN-US">)</span>河南商丘睢县人，<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年因村里土地问题走上维权之路。孟晓东经常参加公益活动，如参与过河南反平坟、为河南许昌被强拆户李建国呼吁等维权活动。曾在于世文、陈卫夫妇发起的六四公祭有签名。因维权多次被抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日，孟晓东被河南睢县公安局以涉嫌寻衅滋事罪刑事拘留，现羁押于河南商丘睢县看守所。随后被批准逮捕。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月底开庭，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，河南省商丘市睢县法院一审以“寻衅滋事罪”判处孟跟东有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>个月。孟跟东目前被羁押在商丘市睢县看守所内。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">莫伟秋：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">天津市宁河区法轮功学员天津市宁河区廉庄乡廉庄村人，与丈夫李广远于一九九七年开始修炼法轮功。自<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年以来，夫妇俩多次被中共非法关押、劳教并被非法判刑，在被非法审判和监禁期间，夫妇俩多次遭到毒打和酷刑折磨。莫伟秋因控告江泽民，于<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日被绑架，再次被判<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年半。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">牟永霞：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">女，<span lang="EN-US">1948</span>年生，大庆市退休教师、法轮功学员。因坚持修炼法轮功，<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日深夜被抓捕，被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，在黑龙江省女子监狱遭受迫害，被折磨得身体极度衰弱，手脚麻木，经常头晕。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日牟永霞被哈尔滨市铁路公安处便衣警察抓捕抄家。牟永霞老人被关押在哈尔滨市第二看守所，绝食抗议抓捕、关押，身体状况被迫害得虚弱，看守所强行给<span lang="EN-US">72</span>岁的牟永霞老人灌食、灌药，进行人身及精神折磨。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月牟永霞老人被大庆市法院判<span lang="EN-US">6</span>年。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">穆塔力浦•伊明（维吾尔）：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">1988</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日出生，新疆维吾尔自治区和田市洛浦县人，维吾尔族名<span lang="EN-US">Mtuellip<span style="mso-spacerun: yes;">&nbsp; </span>Imin</span>，原中央民族大学英语专业本科毕业生，土耳其伊斯坦布尔大学社会学在读硕士留学生，中国在押政治犯。曾于<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年在中央民族大学攻读英语翻译专业，<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月毕业后又成功申请到土耳其国家奖学金项目（<span lang="EN-US">Turkish Scholarships</span>），遂于<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月前往土耳其伊斯坦布尔大学留学，攻读土耳其语（第一年）和社会学硕士（后两年）；<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月初回国度假；但当其于<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日再度前往土耳其继续求学时，在北京首都机场遭到警方拦截，被新疆维吾尔自治区公安厅非法关押<span lang="EN-US">79</span>天，并被胁迫强行修改口供，否则会被“依法判刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>—<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年”；<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日获释后，其计算机、电话、护照及身份证等重要物品仍被新疆警方扣留，致使根本其无法离境求学；无奈之下，其多次上网维权，并举牌要求新疆警方归还所扣之物，且能准予出境继续留学。<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，其在中央民族大学时期的老师、维族学者伊力哈木•土赫提被新疆警方拘捕，其亦于当日被新疆自治区和田市洛浦县警方从家中带走，被以涉嫌“分裂国家罪”刑事拘留；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，因其案件被定为“分裂国家犯罪集团案”而被乌鲁木齐市检察院正式批捕；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日，其案件在乌鲁木齐巿中级法院开庭审理；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，被乌鲁木齐巿中级法院以“积极参与分裂国家犯罪集团罪”重判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">3-8</span>年，最多将于<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日出狱。服刑监狱不详。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">木拉提别克．吾麻尔（哈）：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">新疆伊犁哈萨克自治州巩留县吉尔格郎乡阿勒玛勒村清真寺教长助手。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日，在参加哈萨克族传统节日纳乌鲁斯节后被捕，<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月获悉被判刑<span lang="EN-US">18</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2036</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 22.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">N.<o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">纳杂尔•叶尔江（哈萨克）、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">那仁志、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">乃比江•艾比布拉（维）</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">倪会仙</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">牛腾宇、</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size:
