Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">他与哈纳提别克﹒萨布尔别克、阿尔恒﹒巴杂尔别克、乌木别提﹒卡斯木、哈伊拉提别克﹒木合塔尔汗、沙部旦﹒沙伊合、耶尔肯别克﹒达列力、肯杰别克﹒达列力、玛乌提﹒么斯尔汗都是新疆伊利市哈萨克自治州阿尔泰市巴里巴盖乡人，哈萨克族，穆斯林。其中，纳杂尔﹒叶尔江<span lang="EN-US">26</span>岁，哈纳提别克﹒萨布尔别克<span lang="EN-US">26</span>岁，阿尔恒﹒巴杂尔别克<span lang="EN-US">27</span>岁，乌木别提﹒卡斯木<span lang="EN-US">31</span>岁，哈伊拉提别克﹒木合塔尔汗<span lang="EN-US">37</span>岁，沙部旦﹒沙伊合约<span lang="EN-US">30</span>岁，耶尔肯别克﹒达列力<span lang="EN-US">30</span>岁，肯杰别克﹒达列力<span lang="EN-US">27</span>岁，玛乌提﹒么斯尔汗约<span lang="EN-US">30</span>岁。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">-8</span>月，因他们分别在私下里进行了穆斯林传统常规祷告仪式，而被中共新疆伊犁市哈萨克自治州阿尔泰当局知晓后拘捕，遂很快被阿尔泰市地方法院以“非法从事宗教活动”和“从事宗教极端活动”为由分别判处<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">-6</span>年不等刑期。目前各人具体判刑不详，刑至日期不详，服刑监狱不详，服刑状况及健康程度等不详。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">那仁志：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">江苏省连云港市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日，连云港市海州区公安分局抓捕了法轮功学员刘玉萍、邵世玲、那仁志、熊成霞、周翠萍、马宝玲、高建君、王艾芝、汪宝玉、小周女士、乔老太等十一人。所有人家中都被非法抄了家，警察劫走家中的电脑、手机、光盘、<span lang="EN-US">U</span>盘、电器、钱财、书籍等私人物品。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日，那仁志被开庭，被判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">乃比江•艾比布拉：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">维族，<span lang="EN-US">1983</span>年出生，新疆和田地区洛浦县人，前新疆师范大学、新疆大学和中央民族大学老师，新疆大学优秀本科生导师和研究员，维吾尔语言学教授，中国在押政治犯。早年，曾就读于新疆维吾尔自治区和田师范技术高中中文专业，并于<span lang="EN-US">2002</span>年毕业；<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">-2014</span>年，曾出国留学在德国哥廷根大学攻读博士学位；毕业后又返回新疆；据悉，回国前，曾有多个友人警告他说，“新疆局势正在恶化，建议还是留在德国而不是回国找工作”；但其对此则认为，“若只专注于学术研究，远离社会冲突和其他当局认为有争议的问题，回国仍是安全的”；基于其认为自己回国可以做得更好，且相信通过对维吾尔学生的教授，可以为他们提供更上一层楼的社会机会及工作舞台，<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年，随毅然返回新疆；回国后，曾先后在新疆师范大学、新疆大学和中央民族大学学习与工作；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月，曾因完成一篇题为《汉译佛经中古维吾尔语动词的词典意义》的博士论文，从而获取了<span lang="EN-US">4</span>项研究资助，并在著名学术期刊上发表了<span lang="EN-US">10</span>多篇文章；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月，因中共当局对新疆维吾尔族、哈萨克斯坦族、回族等各族群开始大规模实行“再教育营”（中共称之为“职业技能教育培训机构”）的集中高压管控政策，遂与多位大学其他主要教师及研究人员悉数被警方传唤到所在大学保卫处，并在短暂审讯后被乌鲁木齐市国家安全局警员带走，后送“再教育营”进行洗脑式培训，自此失联；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月，知其被新疆乌鲁木齐市法院秘密重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">15</span>年，罪名不清，服刑截止日期不清；亲友疑其被拘捕判刑与在德国学习期间，其接触了突厥学家阿不都外力，并对维吾尔文化做了大量研究所致。目前服刑监狱不明。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2021/09/15.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2021/09/15.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">南杰顿珠（藏）：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">出生年月不详，四川省甘孜藏族自治州炉霍县人，炉霍寺僧人，中国在押良心犯。由于中共当局在西藏及其周边各省涉藏地区强硬推行“爱国和法制宣传教育”活动，引发多地藏民强烈不满，四川省甘孜州炉霍县藏民于<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日（即当年中国农历新年初一）举行大规模和平示威活动；该活动立即惨遭当地警方严厉的武力镇压和任意抓捕，致使上百藏人被抓，多人被打死打伤；至同年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，共有<span lang="EN-US">36</span>人被中共当局判处<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>个月直至无期徒刑不等的刑期，另有数人被捕后完全失踪；南杰顿珠亦因积极参与抗议示威游行，于<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月被警方以“参与和带头示威活动”为由从当地炉霍寺抓走刑拘；<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，被甘孜藏族自治州炉霍县法院以“炉火示威活动的主要带头人”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">14</span>年。目前在四川省甘孜藏族自治州康定县监狱服刑。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">倪会仙</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">：昆明法轮功学员。女，<span lang="EN-US">1952</span>年生。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月法轮功学员杨靖波、武存仙、倪会仙由于在小区粘贴「法轮大法好！真善忍好！」不干胶，和向住户赠送「天赐洪福」法轮功小册子，被安宁市金方街道办事处不法人员告发，<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日被安宁市国保警察抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日，被西山区法院判处<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>个月有期徒刑，倪会仙刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">宁红</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">：成都市成华区法轮功学员。女，<span lang="EN-US">1960</span>年生，原本是四川人民广播电台记者。在中共迫害法轮功后，宁红因传播法轮功，曾被中共绑架、关押，陷冤狱三年。<span lang="EN-US">2006</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日，宁红因发《九评》光盘，在家中被国安人员和双楠派出所警察绑架，后被非法关押在郫县成都看守所迫害。电台停发了她的工资。<span lang="EN-US">2007</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日，宁红被成都市武侯区法院判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。宁红<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日在成都彭州市传播法轮功资料时，被当地警察抓捕、构陷；<span lang="EN-US">20021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日被彭州市法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，罚金五千元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">宁惠荣：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">男，满族人，基督徒，出生于<span lang="EN-US">1946</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月，原籍北京市，<span lang="EN-US">1966</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月赴新疆“支边”，供职于新疆哈密地区盐化工厂。<span lang="EN-US">2003</span>年，因抗议警察滥权的行为，走上维权之路。<span lang="EN-US">2007</span>年开始赴北京投诉。<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月，向北京市治安总队提交“游行示威”的申请报告，被指控“寻衅滋事”，遭到逮捕。<span lang="EN-US">2010</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月，被新疆地方当局判处三年半监禁，在新疆吐鲁番监狱服刑，因拒不认罪，未获减刑，<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月刑满出狱。宁惠荣于<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日在永定门长途汽车站，被劫访人员从<span lang="EN-US">102</span>路电车上劫走，<span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日被强行带回哈密后，被关押在哈密市公安局派出所，平板电脑、手机、钱包被扣押。宁惠荣因对哈密法院的枉法判决，在向最高人民法院申诉。他们就先抓人，再找罪名，关押至<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日下午，宁惠荣被送到哈密市医院，以治病的名义继续关押，白天二个人看守夜间三个人看守，人身自由被非法限制，至今仍被非法拘禁。后音信全无。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">牛腾宇</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">：<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日出生，山西省晋城市高平市人，有“计算机天才”之称，恶俗维基服务器运维技术人员，“恶俗维基”站长，“恶俗维基网站恶势力犯罪集团案”主要受害人，在押中国政治犯。自<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年起，中国大陆及海外有网友开始频繁尝试搭建和运作被称为“恶俗圈”的网络平台，其中“恶俗维基”、“支那维基”和“红岸基金会”三大网站最为知名；此期间，因其对计算机技术的痴迷与天赋，以及网站宗旨是“揭露并记录事实”，随加入“恶俗维基”网站，并成为该网站技术维护员及站长；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年，曾因多家“恶俗圈”网站频发习近平及家人、和中共高官及家属的户籍和照片等信息，其所在“恶俗维基”网站亦将此类信息挂于网上，遂引发中共当局的极端不满与监控；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，又因其在香港爆发“反送中”大游行之后，与“恶俗维基”创办人肖彦锐相约前去香港，对香港大游行进行围观了解，返回后虽又于同年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月初至<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日到日本一游，但回国一周后；<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，其网站全部会员尽被各地警方突然抓捕，其亦被广东省茂名市警方抓捕，并遭毒打；同年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日，被以涉嫌“帮助信息网络犯罪活动罪”刑拘，关押于茂名市第一看守所；同年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日，被茂名市检察院以同罪名予以批捕，指控其曾在恶俗维基网上“共发表评论<span lang="EN-US">8</span>条，上传图片<span lang="EN-US">20</span>张，共有<span lang="EN-US">748</span>条的用户贡献，其本人有<span lang="EN-US">285</span>条贡献值”等讯息，散布虚假信息，恶毒攻击、诋毁政府和国家领导人及其家属形象等，是“恶俗维基网站恶势力犯罪集团案”主犯，故而应予逮捕和判刑；同年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日，经茂名市检察院批准被延长侦查羁押期限<span lang="EN-US">1</span>个月；<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，又被广东省佛山市警方以涉嫌“颠覆国家政权罪”被指定监视居住，并转关至佛山市南海区看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，其被解除被指定监视居住，同日又被茂名市警方再次逮捕；同年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日，其一行<span lang="EN-US">24</span>人“涉恶势力犯罪集团案”在广东省茂名市法院开庭受审，至<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日，其案<span lang="EN-US">24</span>人均被宣判，其中，其被以“寻衅滋事罪”（判<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年）、“侵犯个人信息罪”（判<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年）、“非法经营罪”（判<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年），最终决定执行有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">14</span>年，并处罚金人民币<span lang="EN-US">13</span>万；其等均表不服，立刻上诉；据悉，其被重判与曾发布中共高层个人信息、镇压香港及新疆等内容有关，且二审法院拟对其速审速决，极有可能维持原判，后二审果然维持原判；另据悉，<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日到<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日期间，为令其屈打成招，曾遭长期刑讯逼供，被吊打致残；刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2033</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日。先被羁押于茂名市第一看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月后被送到了广东省肇庆市四会监狱。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">努尔哈因﹒木哈麦提沙尔（哈萨克）：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">新疆伊利市哈萨克自治州阿尔泰市人，<span lang="EN-US">60</span>岁左右，哈萨克族，穆斯林。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">-8</span>月，中共新疆伊犁哈萨克自治州当局判处了一批穆斯林仪式祷告者，指控其因非法从事了穆斯林式常规祷告仪式，涉嫌法宗教活动或极端宗教活动。其中，努尔哈因﹒木哈麦提沙尔因在家里存有《古兰经》，被警方搜出，随被抓捕，现已被哈萨克自治州法院以“从事极端宗教活动”等为由秘密判刑<span lang="EN-US">6</span>年。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">努尔兰：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">全名是哈德力别克·努尔兰。<span lang="EN-US">1990</span>年代出生，新疆维吾尔自治区阿尔泰地区青河县查干郭勒乡人，哈萨克斯坦族，穆斯林，乌鲁木齐市酷巴巴网络科技有限公司创办人，企业家，中国在押良心犯。早期曾就读于东北大学，<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年毕业；<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年，曾前往新疆乌鲁木齐市创业，后创办酷巴巴网络科技有限公司；<span lang="EN-US"> 2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，曾因宗教信仰而做礼拜（即穆斯林进行敬拜时的祷告方式），被阿尔泰地区青河县当局很快知晓，随被青河县警方带走拘留，并被送进“再教育营”进行洗脑式教育，自此失联；因其在“再教育营”拒绝接受洗脑教育，遂被警方以“从事非法宗教活动”为罪由转为正式逮捕；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月，被新疆维吾尔自治区阿尔泰地区青河县法院重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2028</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月；据悉，其被判刑前后，家属均未收到任何法律文书，家属欲为其聘请辩护律师遭拒，探视权被剥夺，至今不让会面。目前在新疆克拉玛依市监狱服刑。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 22.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">O</span></b><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 22.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">．<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">欧彪峰、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">欧道齐、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">欧彪峰：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1980</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日出生，湖南省株洲市人，人称“小彪”，湖南省宁乡市黑金时代小区居民，维权公民，公民记者，“公民运动”践行者，中国在押政治犯。近年来，曾因积极参与公民维权活动，经常发布被中共当局打压的公民行动者的第一手信息，随遭湖南省当局的维稳监控；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月及<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月，曾因为公开声援许志永和常玮平等良心犯而被当地警方传唤；同年，曾因声援香港反送中运动，并在香港著名媒体大亨、社会活动家黎智英被抓捕后，公开表态支持黎智英及香港《苹果日报》，而遭湖南警方多次警告，并被威胁、暗示当局正在搜寻对其实施抓捕的证据；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日，因关注并协助曾于<span lang="EN-US">2018 </span>年在上海街头向习近平肖像泼墨而被“维稳”（即被当局非法关进精神病医院）的“泼墨女孩”董瑶琼，在推特上发求救呼吁，随立遭当局的严厉打压，被湖南省株洲市芦淞区警方从在宁乡市的家中带走传唤；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日，被以“寻衅滋事”罪由处行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">15</span>天，其家被查抄；同年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日，又被株洲市芦淞区警方以涉嫌“颠覆国家政权罪”转为指定居所监视居住；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日期满后转株洲市第一看守所关押。欧彪峰于<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日经株洲市检察院批准遭湖南株洲市公安局正式逮捕。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">欧道齐：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">湖南省怀化市沅陵县官庄镇人，现居长沙开办少儿培训中心。年约<span lang="EN-US">40</span>岁。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>、<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日间被警方带走，罪名为“寻衅滋事”。欧道齐在长沙的培训机构与铺面也被查封。知情人说，<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日，欧道齐所在的怀化地区老乡群中一网名为“糟老头子”的网友在聊天过程中以一句“习近平上台搞什么都犯法”，来表达对现实社会风声鹤唳草木皆兵的统治手法不满，其后该名友遭到警方抓捕，并有知情群员将警方的核查通报上传至该群组。随后多名网友将该图片转发到其他社交平台，其中就包括欧道齐。据称欧道齐将图片上传发布在推特后不久便被警方发现，并根据<span lang="EN-US">IP</span>地址将其拘捕。后音信全无。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 22.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">P</span></b><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">．<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">潘培德</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">潘学明</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、潘艳春、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">潘玉峰</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">兀亚莉、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">裴玉凤、裴玉贤</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;">彭彪、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">彭石清、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">彭文缄、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">彭宇华、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">朴顺南（朝鲜族）、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">普化（藏）、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">卜宝玲、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">潘培德：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1956</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年生，退休工人，广东省茂名市电白区法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日下午<span lang="EN-US">4</span>点左右，潘培德在电白水东家里，警察对潘培德实施抓捕、抄家；下午<span lang="EN-US">6</span>点左右，又把他关押到米粮村老家抄家； 第<span lang="EN-US">2</span>天，即<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日下午，潘培德被刑事拘留。并被关押到茂名市第<span lang="EN-US">1</span>看守所关押。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日被茂名市茂南区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">潘学明：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">辽宁大连市甘井子区法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">1957</span>年生。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月大连市政法委、六一零借口“七十年大庆”维稳，操控国保大队等长期对法轮功学员监视、监听、跟踪，于<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日抓捕了至少大连七位法轮功学员。当天早晨，潘学明在家中被凌水派出所警察抓捕、抄家，抢劫走电脑、打印机、大法书籍。因身体状况，监狱不收，潘学明至今仍被羁押在大连姚家看守所。潘学明被关在看守所<span lang="EN-US">4-12</span>监室，吃喝拉撒睡都在监室。身陷囹圄，暗无天日的铁窗生活，加之办案人员的刑讯逼供，导致潘学明身体出现严重病态，经常咳嗽，肺部呼吸困难。在不适合羁押的情况下，仍遭高新园区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 351.75pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">潘艳春：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">辽宁大连市法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">1970</span>年生。大连市甘井子区法轮功学员，在新疆石河子做生意，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日发放法轮功资料，后被警察抓捕，被关押在新疆石河子第一看守所。在后被非法判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年（刑期<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日起至<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日）。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">潘玉峰：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">辽宁朝阳市两法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日下午，潘玉峰在家中被北塔分局警察抓捕。潘玉峰是位难得的孝子，家中老母亲患老年痴呆，生活不能自理，一直由潘玉峰照顾。自潘玉峰被绑架后，老人无人照顾，很快消瘦了很多，在潘玉峰绑架近一年后老人悲苦离开人世，临终都未见到儿子一面。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日，潘玉峰案开庭，律师做无罪辩护。后得知潘玉峰被双塔法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">兀亚莉：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">女，<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年五十七岁，一九九九年四月开始修炼法轮功。曾被非法抄家五次、拘留四次、被洗脑班拘禁一次、劳教两年，<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日被绑架、冤判<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，长期被监视居住，遭受非法开除公职等迫害。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月上旬，兀亚莉被汉中市汉台区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">裴玉凤：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">黑龙江安达市女法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日晚赵秀芝、裴玉凤、陈景捷<span lang="EN-US">3</span>位法轮功学员被警察等非法闯入各自的家中抓捕的。赵秀芝、裴玉凤、陈景捷被关押在安达看守所。后获悉裴玉凤被判刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年半，陈景捷被判刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年半。赵秀芝被判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">裴玉贤：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">河北秦皇岛法轮功学员。其丈夫李彦春也是法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日，因其夫妇二人到秦皇岛市卢龙县散发法轮功宣传挂历，被恶人告发，随被卢龙县双望派出所警方抓捕，且被戴手铐、脚镣等，审讯时，惨遭殴打和刑讯逼供；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日，其夫妇二人涉邪教案被卢龙县警方递交到卢龙县检察院，后被卢龙县检察院以涉嫌邪教罪予以正式批捕；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日，其案在秦皇岛市昌黎县法院开庭受理；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日，被河北省秦皇岛市昌黎县法院一审以“利用邪教组织破坏法律实施罪”重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，并处罚金<span lang="EN-US">2</span>万元，后因身体极差原因被准予保外就医；其妻裴玉贤亦被以同罪名判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，并处罚金<span lang="EN-US">5</span>千元；二人不服判决，当庭均表示上诉；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日，其被秦皇岛市卢龙县双望派出所警方再次收监逮捕，旋即被送往监狱接续服刑；其妻裴玉贤亦在此前被送河北省石家庄女子监狱服刑。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2021/09/76.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2021/09/76.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;">彭彪：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">贵州省六盘水市盘州市城关镇法轮功学员。彭彪于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日，被盘州市公安局绑架，而后被送至六盘水市第二看守所关押、构陷迫害。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日左右，由六盘水市第二看守所通知，彭彪被六盘水市中级法院判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。现彭彪被非法关押在贵州省都匀监狱六监区迫害。据悉彭彪现被<span lang="EN-US">4</span>个刑事犯包夹迫害。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">彭石清：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">湖南省湘潭市人，湘潭市岳塘区板塘花苑居民小区居民，某工厂木工，法轮功信仰者，良心犯。因笃信法轮功而曾被当局多次抓捕关押，甚至曾被枉判<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年，并先后在沅江赤山监狱、常德津市监狱服刑，备受酷刑虐待。<a name="_Hlk512558029">出狱后，因其依然坚持信仰不变，遂遭当局更严厉监控打压。</a><span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日早，突然被湘潭市公安高新分局双马派出所警方数十人闯入家中，将其夫妇二人双双抓走，随后家被查抄，搜走相关法轮功资料数份，并将其所有存折、银行卡、社保卡、身份证等私人物品也一并搜走。当日其即被送往湘潭市看守所关押。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，其妻熊春霞在被索要了<span lang="EN-US">3000</span>元保释金后准予释放回家，而其竟被以涉邪教罪转正式批捕，被指控因制作和发放法轮功真相资料、印制有法轮功真相内容的人民币，以及发送法轮功真相内容短信等，因此违反了相关法律。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日，其案在看守所内被湘潭市岳塘区法院秘密开庭，最终其被一审以“组织、利用邪教组织破坏法律实施罪”重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">9</span>年。目前被关押在湘潭市看守所。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">彭文缄：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">广东揭阳市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">1960</span>年代生人。家住揭阳市东阳办事处东山村。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日下午，揭阳市榕城区公安分局国保大队伙同揭阳市东阳派出所，到黄建民家进行抓捕抄家。因黄建民在自己家开了商店，经常收到一些真相币，此次抄家抄到了真相币，就成了国保抓捕黄建民的冠冕堂皇的借口了。后黄建民彭文缄夫妇被关押揭阳市看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日，黄建民被判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年、妻子彭文缄被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">.</span>刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">彭宇华：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">1980</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日出生，湖北省籍人，理财经理，人权活动者。自<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年以来，因其创建了“两岸牵手”、“围观中国”、“围观华南”等系列<span lang="EN-US">QQ</span>群，并与李明哲等数十名境内外非政府组织成员及人权活动者，成立了旨在建立新型民主制度和进行中国大陆人权活动的“梅花公司”，遂被中共警方跟踪、监控。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日被湖南省长沙市国家安全局以涉嫌“颠覆国家政权罪”刑事拘留；同年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日，被长沙市检察院以同罪名正式批捕，同日被长沙市警方正式逮捕，并指控其创建了系列<span lang="EN-US">QQ</span>群，炒作近年来大陆发生的热点事件，发布诋毁、攻击政府部门和大陆制度的言论，成立了“旨在颠覆大陆政权、推翻大陆基本政治制度的组织<span lang="EN-US">'</span>梅花公司<span lang="EN-US">'</span>”，制定了组织纲领，确定了组织框架和人员细致分工，组织<span lang="EN-US">100</span>万成员插手围观所谓热点事件，触犯了中国法律。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日其案在岳阳市中级法院开庭受审，同年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日被该法院以“颠覆国家政权罪”判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年，剥权<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年。对于一审他表示服从判决。目前被羁押于湖南省岳阳市看守所。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">朴顺南（朝鲜）：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">女，<span lang="EN-US">1962</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日出生，辽宁省辽阳市人，朝鲜族，辽阳市朝光村基督教家庭教会负责人，中国在押良心犯。因其教会为基督教家庭教会，且不愿到中共当局指定的“三自”教会敬拜、聚会，遂遭致当局的严打惩罚；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，其被辽阳市太子河区警方突然以涉嫌“非法经营罪”抓捕刑拘，并被指控教会内部使用了基督徒信仰灵修崇拜书籍及相关印刷品，并在教会的便利店销往其他省市，属于非法买卖行为；同年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日被转正式逮捕；<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日被辽宁省辽阳市太子河区法院以“非法经营罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年。目前被羁押于辽阳市看守所。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">普化（藏）：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">青海省黄南州同仁县多哇乡人，藏族人权捍卫者。<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月，中共<span lang="EN-US">18</span>大召开前夕、期间及之后，在藏区多地仅一个月内共发生了<span lang="EN-US">28</span>起自焚事件，当时同仁县就有<span lang="EN-US">9</span>位藏人自焚，其中多哇乡<span lang="EN-US">5</span>人自焚，均身亡。事发后，中共当局很快成立了青海省公安厅驻黄南州系列自焚案件专案组，并以涉嫌“散布自焚者照片并在照片上写下自焚者遗言”、“参与反政府示威抗议活动”等罪，抓捕藏民<span lang="EN-US">70</span>人。之后，有<span lang="EN-US">52</span>人被刑拘，有<span lang="EN-US">12</span>人被逮捕，普化即是其中宣布被正式逮捕者之一。<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，其多人在黄南州同仁县法院被宣判，普化被以不知名罪名重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">13</span>年。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">卜宝玲：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">女、<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">70</span>岁，黑龙江哈尔滨法轮功学员。哈尔滨市哈尔滨市依兰县公安局<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日下午对依兰县、佳木斯市桦川县两地法轮功学员实施绑架，到<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日共有<span lang="EN-US">29</span>人被绑架，其中十四名法轮功学员宋玉芝、施凤香、施凤兰、王云杰、周妍、邓术梅、宋孔华、武桂琴、卜宝玲、夏桂华、唐立飞、姚怀英、康艳玲、庞秀贤，与薛宏亮（未修炼法轮功）被长期关押构陷，<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日遭依兰县法院庭审。卜宝玲被判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，处罚金<span lang="EN-US">3</span>万元，刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 22.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">Q</span></b><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">． <span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">齐红玉、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">齐晓东、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">戚凤珍</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">恰特合•达吾列提（哈）、</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">千根太、</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">强巴格勒（藏）、强巴旺秋（藏）、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">乔华荣、<span style="mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">乔莲红</span>、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">乔向阳、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">秦丽杰、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">秦莲玉、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">秦雪美</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、秦永敏、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">覃德富、覃永沛、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">邱安、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">邱汉浓、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">邱林、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">曲风荣、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">曲红、曲嘉唯色（藏）、曲桑嘉措（藏）。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">齐红玉：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">黑龙江省双鸭山市集贤县法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日<span lang="EN-US">10</span>点左右，集贤县法轮功学员齐红玉女士在街上讲真相时，被不明真相世人诬告，被抓捕到前进派出所。下午三点多，国保大队长冯树斌等人，带着开锁人员打开齐红玉家门抄家，当晚把齐红玉送进双鸭山市看守所。后在未通知家人的情况下，集贤县法院非法对齐红玉开庭，判<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年有期徒刑。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">齐晓东：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1996</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日出生，吉林省长春市宽城区人，北京市海淀区双榆树北路<span lang="EN-US">6</span>号院<span lang="EN-US">2</span>号楼<span lang="EN-US">3</span>单元<span lang="EN-US">1</span>层<span lang="EN-US">101</span>号居民，“恶俗维基”及“支纳维基”二网站组建人（之一），“恶俗维基网站恶势力犯罪集团案”受害人之一，中国在押政治犯。自<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年起，中国大陆及海外有网友开始频繁尝试搭建和运作被称为“恶俗圈”的网络平台，其中“恶俗维基”、“支那维基”和“红岸基金会”三大网站最为知名；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年至<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年期间，曾因与旅居日本的网络达人肖彦锐及香港即可科技有限公司部分员工等多人，共同参与组建“恶俗维基”、“支那维基”二网站，并设置创始人、行政员、管理员、站长、注册用户等<span lang="EN-US">5</span>个层级，多个规章制度和使用多个电报群管理成员等，而受到合作友人地好评；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年，曾因多家“恶俗圈”网站频发习近平之女习明泽、姐夫邓家贵的个人信息（含户籍和照片等信息），其所在“恶俗维基”网和“支那维基”网亦将此类信息挂于网上；遂遭到中共当局的极度不满与强烈打击；同年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月—<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月，公安部迅速成立项目组，在全国对其网站会员实施大抓捕，后经严格审讯发觉他们基本无罪，故而各地警方纷纷将其释放，唯广东省茂名市警方想立功，宣称要给中共建政<span lang="EN-US">70</span>周年献大礼，遂移花接木嫁祸“恶俗维基”，把其全部会员（含其在内）抓捕，并上报公安部称“破获了一起与反华势力相勾结的恶势力集团大案”；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日，其被以涉嫌“帮助信息网络犯罪活动罪”抓捕刑拘，同年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，被转正式逮捕；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月和<span lang="EN-US"> 5</span>月，因资料不全，其案被茂名市检察院两次退侦；同年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月和<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月，侦查机关对其案件重新提起公诉，但仍被当地检察院三次延长审查起诉期限；同年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日，其一行<span lang="EN-US">24</span>人“涉恶势力犯罪集团案”在广东省茂名市茂南区法院开庭受审；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日，其案<span lang="EN-US">24</span>人均被宣判，其中，因其在此前同意“使用认罪认罚程序审理”，遂最终被一审以“寻衅滋事罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日；其表示不服，上诉；二审维持原判。目前被羁押于佛山市南海区看守所。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">戚凤珍：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">吉林白城市法轮功学员，女。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日发放法轮功资料，被白城市公安局抓捕，被关押在白城市看守所。看守所不让家属见面，家属担忧戚凤珍的身体情况。在被非法关押、被构陷大半年后，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年过年前夕，被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年。戚凤珍刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">恰特合·达吾列提（哈）：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1988</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日出生，新疆维吾尔自治区伊犁哈萨克斯坦自治州人，伊犁哈萨克斯坦自治州察布查尔锡伯自治县捷仁布拉克镇<span lang="EN-US">67</span>团<span lang="EN-US">8</span>连哈萨克族公民，中国在押良心犯。被抓捕前，一直是遵纪守法的好公民，并因身有严重疾患长期与病魔做着殊死搏斗；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日，曾被新疆建设兵团农四师医院诊断为慢性粒细胞白血病；后因病情严重，于<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日被转到新疆医科大学第一附属医院住院治疗<span lang="EN-US">8</span>天；<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年，曾两度前往北京市住院治疗，但又因无力承担高昂的治疗费用<span lang="EN-US">,</span>只能中途放弃治疗；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，其病情再次复发，不得不在新疆医科大学第一附属医院住院治疗，每月药费<span lang="EN-US">3</span>万元；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日，恰特合·达吾列提被伊犁州察布查尔锡伯自治县警方突然以不明罪由抓捕，被送入当地“教育培训中心”（又称“再教育营”）接受中共洗脑式教育；同年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日，旋即被察布查尔锡伯自治县检察院予以批捕；<span lang="EN-US"> 2019</span>年，被伊犁哈萨克斯坦自治州察布查尔锡伯自治县法院以不明罪名重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">19</span>年，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2037</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日； 据悉，其被判刑前因身患白血病严重，医生建议做干细胞移植手术，但向狱方申请保外就医以求手术治疗，遭拒；又悉，因其被抓捕判刑，其家人（妻子、两个孩子及其母亲）生活陷入困境。 目前疑似在新疆伊犁哈萨克斯坦自治州新源监狱服刑。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">千根泰<span lang="EN-US">:</span></span></b><span lang="EN-US"> </span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">吉林省长春市二道区朝鲜族法轮功学员。千根太、张星姬夫妇在修炼法轮功前，曾在长春市二道区创办食品厂，一九九九年七月中共开始迫害法轮功后，很多法轮功学员进京和平请愿，有的被迫害致流离失所、无家可归。千根太、张星姬夫妇收留几位法轮功学员，被中共发现，后来被迫关闭了食品厂。中共警察上门骚扰不断，千根太、张星姬夫妇不得不将家里的三套房子变卖，被迫流离失所。后遭劳教。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月下旬，千根泰、张星姬夫妇被长春市二道区公安分局和顺街派出所警察抓捕、关押。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月获悉，千根泰、张星姬夫妇被长春市二道区法院枉判<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年半。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">强巴格勒</span></b><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">（藏）</span></b><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">四川省甘孜藏族羌族自治区州阿坝县尼措寺僧人，<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">23</span>岁，是道孚县人。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日傍晚<span lang="EN-US">8</span>点多钟，强巴格勒在前往附近一佛塔转经途中，突然被中共公安人员拘捕。被指在僧舍中挂有西藏国旗，并曾表露想要为西藏政教事业而自焚的念头。后音信全无。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">强巴旺秋（藏）</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">:1959</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年出生，西藏自治区边波隆都县索托乡（注：此为藏语拼音名，汉语地名不明，疑为拉萨市附近某县<span lang="EN-US">/</span>乡）人，藏名<span lang="EN-US">Jampel Wangchuk</span>，俗名次培（<span lang="EN-US">Tsephel</span>），拉萨市哲蚌寺洛色林僧院高级僧人、纪律纠察僧官，学者僧侣，中国在押良心犯。自幼成为僧侣，并在西藏拉萨市哲蚌寺所在僧侣学院进修学习；后因长期师从藏族著名佛学教师兰林仁波切（<span lang="EN-US">Lamrim<span style="mso-spacerun: yes;">&nbsp; </span>Rinpoche</span>），成为其身边主要弟子，随拥有深厚博学的藏传佛学知识，且被哲蚌寺洛色林僧院确定为高级僧人及纪律纠察僧官；<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月，西藏发生大规模以僧侣为主体的抗议示威活动，以表达对中共当局长期压制、管控藏区人民的不满；他们强烈呼吁中共当局要实现（或兑现）藏民族“自治独立”，并要求让达赖喇嘛回国返乡，对藏区进行自治管理等政治诉求；针对此，同年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，拉萨的哲蚌寺约有<span lang="EN-US">350</span>名僧侣亦本着推动实现这些诉求，发起进一步的大规模抗议活动，使事态迅速波及到整个拉萨市区，甚至四川及青海藏区；对于此次抗议行动，中共警方随即采取了制止行为，但又因中共手段过于极端，导致双方发生对峙冲突，期间部分僧人被抓；<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日，其被拉萨市警方突然以涉嫌“抗议活动”刑拘，自此失联；另有同寺僧侣好友贡觉尼玛、阿旺觉尼亦被拘捕；后其被拉萨市警方正式逮捕，理由是虽未参加当时的抗议示威，但因未能阻止所在寺庙僧人举行大规模抗议行动，遂属于违规或违反相关管理条例行为；<span lang="EN-US">2010</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月，在超期关押<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年之久后，终被拉萨市中级法院秘密重判无期徒刑，罪名不详；据悉，其辩护权遭剥夺，至今其在狱中健康状况及所处具体环境等均无下落。目前疑似在拉萨曲水监狱服刑。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><a name="_Hlk54972303"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">乔华荣<span lang="EN-US">:</span></span></b></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk54972303;"></span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">乔华荣、赵根法、黄春玲、刘洪兰四人都是山东省曲阜市的法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日，黄春玲在刘洪兰家做客，赵根法、乔华荣夫妻去看她们，刚坐下还没说几句话，曲阜市国保大队人员就进入刘洪兰家，以「非法集会、集体学法」等罪名，将他们抓捕至书院派出所，另外以「把你的包拿过来看一下」为由将赵根法钥匙夺走，在赵根法、乔华荣夫妻二人都不在场、家中无人的情况下抄家，将法轮功书籍、手机、光盘、笔记本计算机、内存卡、</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">U</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">盘等几十件物品劫走。第二天，即<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日，赵根法被关押在曲阜市拘留所；乔华荣、刘洪兰被送往济宁市看守所进行关押；黄春玲被关押在泗水县拘留所。后赵根法、黄春玲、刘洪兰、乔华荣，被抓捕、关押一年多，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日遭济宁市任城区法院庭审，赵根法被判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年半，黄春玲、刘洪兰被判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>个月，乔华荣被判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。四人都被非法罚款一万元。乔华荣刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">乔莲红：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">广州<span lang="EN-US">11.12</span>大抓捕被抓人员。广州国安局以颠覆国家政权为由，于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日在广州对民运人士进行了大抓捕，目前已有四人被抓捕，分别是：范一平、范文成、赖见君、乔莲红。被抓后，即遭指定监视居住，罪名是颠覆国家政权。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">乔向阳：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">河南新郑市法轮功信徒、残疾人。家住新郑市龙湖镇沙窝李村，<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日下午被新郑市警方以“扫黑除恶”的名义抓捕，家中私人物品被掠走。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日，新郑市法院对乔向阳判刑<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">秦丽杰：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">陕西宝鸡石油机械厂法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日下午，宝鸡市金台公安分局出动了多辆警车、几十个警察，抓捕了宝鸡石油机械厂的八名法轮功学员及家属。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日，秦丽杰、李宝莲、寇爱梅三人被关押到宝鸡第二看守所非法逮捕、关押，其他人已于<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日被释放回家。后获悉秦丽杰被判<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，寇爱梅被判<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年半，李宝莲被判<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>个月。秦丽杰刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">秦莲玉：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">浙江宁波市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日，宁波市二十多名法轮功学员被当局绑架，遭受不同程度的迫害，秦莲玉被关押在宁波市看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日，在宁波市镇海区法院，秦莲玉案第二次被开庭，其被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，罚款六千元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">秦雪美：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">重庆法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日重庆<span lang="EN-US">5</span>名法轮功学员李嘉惠、张盛全、李玉华、高洪伟、秦雪美被抓捕，两年多后<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月才获悉已经被判刑。秦雪美<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，罚金<span lang="EN-US">4</span>千元。张盛全、李嘉惠，被枉判<span lang="EN-US">9</span>年，勒索罚金<span lang="EN-US">1</span>万元；李玉华<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，罚金<span lang="EN-US">8</span>千元，监外执行；高洪伟<span lang="EN-US">6</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，罚金<span lang="EN-US">5</span>千元；秦雪美刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">秦永敏：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">1953</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日出生，湖北省鄂州市籍人，早年为湖北省武汉钢铁公司冷轧厂职工，著名民间政治学者、自由撰稿人，中国民主党湖北省党部重要创始人，“中国人权观察”（注册中）理事长、“玫瑰中国团队”负责人，著名人权活动家，中国在押政治犯。<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日，其被湖北省当局再度非法抓捕，罪由是“接受外媒采访及写文章过多”，其妻亦遭当局拘押、失联；<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日获悉，其已被湖北省武汉市警方以涉嫌“煽动颠覆国家政权罪”秘密羁押。现得知被羁押于武汉市第二看守所，案子在检察院。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日第一次获律师会见，状态良好。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">2018</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日上午在武汉中级法院三号审判庭公开宣判。秦永敏被以颠覆政权罪判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">13</span>年，剥夺政治权利<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。刑期自<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日起至<span lang="EN-US">2028</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日止。</span><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">覃德富：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">四川省人，基督徒，成都秋雨圣约归正家庭教会长老，<span lang="EN-US">12</span>·<span lang="EN-US">9</span>成都秋雨教案当事人之一，中国在押良心犯。近年来受洗皈依基督教，后在成都秋雨圣约家庭教会当长老；因与牧师王怡等众神职人员及信徒多次在成都市街头宣传基督教福音，并坚持其所在教会以“家庭教会”模式为主聚会，拒绝参加中共认可的“三自教会”，遂遭中共当局严酷打压；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，其在<span lang="EN-US">12</span>·<span lang="EN-US">9</span>秋雨教案大抓捕中被成都市青羊区警方以涉嫌“非法经营罪”刑拘；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日，被以“非法经营罪”判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">覃永沛：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">广西人权律师。覃永沛是在<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月被注销律师牌照。由他主持，曾代理过不少维权案件的”百举鸣律师事务所”，被勒令解散后，转为法律咨询公司的形式，继续提供法律服务。覃永沛也连同多名维权律师，成立“中国律师后俱乐部”。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月末，覃永沛所属原律师事务所律师陈家鸿被玉林警方拘留，罪名为“煽动颠覆国家政权罪”。当时覃永沛曾积极作出声援及呼吁放人，目前陈家鸿律师尚在羁押。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日傍晚五点左右，南宁警方十数人闯入原百举鸣律师事务所（现百永鸣法律咨询服务有限公司）办公室，将该所原主任、人权律师后覃永沛控制并带走，同时覃的办公室被警方查封。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日，广西人权律师覃永沛被指涉煽动颠覆国家政权罪遭刑事拘留。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月案件移送检察院审查起诉。已经进入审判阶段，未开庭。现关押在南宁第一看守所。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">邱安：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">云南昆明市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年，又在店铺被人举报宣传法轮功及发放<span lang="EN-US">5</span>本小册子，并当场查获包中书籍<span lang="EN-US">1</span>本，小册子<span lang="EN-US">9</span>本、护身符<span lang="EN-US">4</span>个。因此要求法院从重处罚。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日下午，邱安被<span lang="EN-US">5</span>华法院开庭判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，罚款<span lang="EN-US">5</span>千；刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US">11</span>日下午六点多钟将邱汉浓抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日被判<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>个月，并勒索罚钱<span lang="EN-US">3000</span>元。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">邱林：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日下午<span lang="EN-US">3</span>点左右，邱林在蛟河夜市给以位公安退休老人讲法轮功时，被老人恶意举报，遭长安街道派出所警察抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，吉林省舒兰市法院，在没有通知家属的情况下，通过远程视频开庭，以「迷信组织会道门，破坏法律实施罪」判刑蛟河市法轮功学员邱林<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，罚金两千元。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">曲风荣：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font:
