mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">沈良庆：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">沈良庆系安徽合肥人，<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">57</span>岁。中国著名异议人士，曾任职于安徽检察院。早在<span lang="EN-US">1984</span>年，他便投身民主运动，创办民间刊物《大学生与社会》，宣扬自由人权与普世价值。因早年参与<span lang="EN-US">89</span>学运，<span lang="EN-US">1992</span>年被合肥法院以“煽动颠覆国家政权罪”被判刑一年半。 沈良庆刚直不阿，敢说敢言，常年在<span lang="EN-US">Twitter</span>上针砭时弊。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日沈良庆遭合肥公安以涉嫌寻衅滋事罪刑事拘留。同年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，被合肥市包河区警方以同罪由转正式逮捕；据悉，其在抓捕审讯过程中，遭到戴黑头套、<span lang="EN-US">24</span>小时禁吃喝、禁去厕所，并被疲劳审讯等酷刑。沈良庆案件<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日开庭后，一直没有判决，律师电话询问多次，没有得到正面回应。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月，律师在看守所会见了沈先生，得知他的身体目前状况不好。近两年的羁押对他身体造成了损害。尤其是他的左手掌，以前做过手术，目前手掌内部复发炎症，手掌肿胀可见。他自述，痛感很强，靠吃消炎药支撑。律师随即把这个情况与审判法官进行了沟通，再次申请取保候审。法院还没有正面回复。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2021</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日沈良庆被合肥市包河区法院宣判寻衅滋事罪名成立，被判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日。</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">现被羁押在合肥看守所。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2021/11/2-3.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2021/11/2-3.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">沈忠勤：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">辽宁省沈阳市沈河区法轮功学员。女，<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">64</span>岁。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日去沈北新区蒲河镇大集买东西，刚到那里不一会儿，被辉山派出所警察殴打绑架。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日被沈阳市沈北新区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">司太安</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">：河南省平顶山市鲁山县法轮功学员，<span lang="EN-US">1952</span>年生，家住河南省平顶山市鲁山县马楼乡虎营村，<span lang="EN-US">1996</span>年开始修炼法轮功。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，马楼派出所警察闯到司太安家实施抓捕，将独自一人在家的司太安押到鲁山县看守所关押。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2020</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，司太安在鲁山县看守所内被鲁山县法院庭审，法官不让家人参加，不许律师做无罪辩护。后被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，并勒索罚金<span lang="EN-US">2</span>千元。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">宋德满<span lang="EN-US">:</span></span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"> </span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">吉林市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，吉林市公安局及下属派出所警察抓捕至少有<span lang="EN-US">21</span>名法轮功学员、二名家属，法轮功学员陈继海、宋德满是其中两位。被关押一年余，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月，陈继海和宋德满分别被判<span lang="EN-US">9</span>年和<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年，现在吉林省第二监狱服刑。宋德满刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">宋桂香：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">山东青岛市胶州七旬法轮功学员。因信仰被迫害多年。<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，宋桂香及家人通过快递分别向北京最高检察院、最高法院邮寄了刑事控告书，控告江泽民发起对法轮功学员的迫害。<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日上午，以阜安派出所负责人想找她们母女“谈话”的名义将宋桂香、李雪骗至派出所，然后羁押于青岛普东看守所进行迫害。<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日，宋桂香被胶州法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年。因身体原因宋桂香于<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日保外就医回家。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月又被送往山东省女子监狱服刑。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">宋国礼：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">甘肃省白银市靖远县法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">64</span>岁。靖远县东湾镇三合村农民，<span lang="EN-US">1998</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月修炼法轮功。因张贴法轮功标语，<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日，宋国礼在公交车上被靖远县<span lang="EN-US">610</span>绑架。后宋国礼被送到靖远县看守所关押。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日被白银法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>个月，勒索罚金八千元，<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日被送到甘肃省大沙坪监狱服刑。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">宋孔华：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">男、<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">58</span>岁，黑龙江哈尔滨法轮功学员。哈尔滨市哈尔滨市依兰县公安局<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日下午对依兰县、佳木斯市桦川县两地法轮功学员实施绑架，到<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日共有<span lang="EN-US">29</span>人被绑架，其中十四名法轮功学员宋玉芝、施凤香、施凤兰、王云杰、周妍、邓术梅、宋孔华、武桂琴、卜宝玲、夏桂华、唐立飞、姚怀英、康艳玲、庞秀贤，与薛宏亮（未修炼法轮功）被长期关押构陷，<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日遭依兰县法院庭审。宋孔华被判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年， 处罚金<span lang="EN-US">3</span>万元，刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">宋彦群：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1971</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年出生于吉林省舒兰市，毕业于长春商业高等专科学校国际贸易系，为人正直，心地善良。她曾任哈尔滨大德日语学校英语教师。<span lang="EN-US">1996</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月修炼法轮功。因坚持修炼法轮功，被劳教迫害；宋彦群与妹妹宋冰均是优秀的专业人才，正值风华正茂、事业有成之时，<span lang="EN-US">2003</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日夜晚又被舒兰市公安局恶警破门而入抓捕、惨无人道的折磨，分别被秘密判刑<span lang="EN-US">12</span>年、<span lang="EN-US">14</span>年，妹妹宋冰<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>十日被迫害致死，年仅<span lang="EN-US">36</span>岁；宋彦群被迫害的骨瘦如柴、生命垂危，<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年保外就医时体重仅剩<span lang="EN-US">80</span>来斤。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日上午<span lang="EN-US">9</span>时许，舒兰市公安局国保大队长董其明<span lang="EN-US">8</span>人来到宋彦群家，问宋彦群：「你给李克强写信了吧！信邮去北京返回来了，信访局查办要抓你。」并拿出吉林省信访局督办文件，让宋彦群念，引诱宋彦群回答他们要的问题，如「你为甚么给李克强写信？」等，整个过程有人录像。晚<span lang="EN-US">6</span>点，北城派出所副所长朱峰来到宋家，将宋彦群抓捕到北城派出所，后关押在吉林市看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，家人被告知，宋彦群被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年半，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">宋宇岑：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1995</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年出生。沈阳市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日，宋宇岑在沈阳医大一院向病人讲法轮功真相，与人分享走出忧郁症的秘诀，遭护士恶告，被保安带到保安室并报警。<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日，宋宇岑被沈阳市和平公安分局警察关入和平区看守所。被抓捕、关押近两年，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日家属得知他被判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">宋玉芝：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">女、<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">65</span>岁，黑龙江哈尔滨法轮功学员。哈尔滨市哈尔滨市依兰县公安局<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日下午对依兰县、佳木斯市桦川县两地法轮功学员实施绑架，到<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日共有<span lang="EN-US">29</span>人被绑架，其中十四名法轮功学员宋玉芝、施凤香、施凤兰、王云杰、周妍、邓术梅、宋孔华、武桂琴、卜宝玲、夏桂华、唐立飞、姚怀英、康艳玲、庞秀贤，与薛宏亮（未修炼法轮功）被长期关押构陷，<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日遭依兰县法院庭审。宋玉芝被判刑<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年， 处罚金<span lang="EN-US">6</span>万<span lang="EN-US">5</span>千元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">宋志刚：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">辽宁省葫芦岛市兴城市人，兴城市农机修造厂职工，法轮功信仰者，良心犯。因手机丢失，被他人拾到后送到公安局，公安局发现他的手机中存有与法轮功有关的内容，随于<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日被新疆阿克陶县公安局拘捕，后被阿克陶县检察院以涉嫌“利用邪教组织破坏法律实施罪”批捕，并被关押在阿克陶县看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月被新疆阿克陶县法院以同罪名枉法重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">14</span>年，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2031</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">宋宗孝（宋有福）<span lang="EN-US">:</span></span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">男，甘肃临夏县新集镇梁家山村法轮功学员，<span lang="EN-US">1941</span>年生。在<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年因写法轮大法标语被抓，被判四年半，在天水监狱遭受迫害。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日（正月初十），临夏县新集派出所警察四人穿着便衣到宋宗孝家骚扰，并撕毁大门上的真相对联。临夏县公安局国保大队伙同新集镇派出所<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月份抓捕了宋宗孝。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月底被判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年半，并处罚金四千元。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">苏东亮</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">：<span lang="EN-US">1981</span>年出生，前陕西省府谷县法院书记员、民事审判第一庭助审员，维权公民，新公民运动参与者。<span lang="EN-US">2007</span>年毕业于西北政法大学之后，<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年，在陕西省府谷县法院参加工作并任书记员；<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年，任民事审判第一庭助理审判员，此期间，一直对现行司法体系的混乱与腐败等问题感到悲凉和无奈，并积极寻求如何改变社会问题的民主之路；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年初，他毅然辞去原有工作，前往广州等地参加民主活动，并与张六毛、项逢选等人结为好友，经常参与围观声援、同城聚餐等活动；<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日与张六毛、项逢选等多人一同被广州市珠海区警方以涉“颠覆国家政权罪”刑拘。一个月后被广州天河区检察院以涉“危害国家安全罪”正式批捕，并被定性为“制造炸弹危害公共安全案”主犯之一；<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日，获悉与其同案的维权公民张六毛在广州第三看守所被酷刑致死，而依然毫无信息，其家人亦因受官方恐吓而拒绝与外界联系。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月得知，其可能已与项逢选一起被广州市中级法院以“危害国家安全案主犯”判刑。目前服刑监狱不详。刑期不详。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">苏坤：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">60</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">多岁，黑龙江省哈尔滨市尚志市苇河镇人，法轮功学员。因信法轮功而屡遭中共<span lang="EN-US">610</span>办公室严厉逼迫打击。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，当二人与法轮功学员革振华一起坐着微型面包车去哈尔滨市尚志市亮河镇挂条幅、散发法轮功宣传资料时，被恶人告发，回来的路上在亚布力镇，被赶来的当地警方围堵抓捕，前挡风玻璃被打碎，车辆被扣押，次日即被警方以涉邪教罪刑事拘留。同年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日二人被转正式逮捕，同时关押在哈尔滨市第二看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日，其案件被尚志市检察院向尚志市法院提起诉讼，并提出对革振华、苏坤冤判<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年<span lang="EN-US">-6</span>年，对王翠娥冤判<span lang="EN-US">2-3</span>年的建议。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日，二人被哈尔滨市尚志市法院以“利用邪教组织破坏法律实施罪”分别枉法重判：苏坤被判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年、罚金<span lang="EN-US">4</span>万，王翠娥被判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年、罚金<span lang="EN-US">1</span>万。二人不服，提起上诉。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，经哈尔滨市中级法院二审重新改判：苏坤被判<span lang="EN-US">6</span>年、罚金<span lang="EN-US">2</span>万，王翠娥被判<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年、罚金<span lang="EN-US">5</span>千。据悉，关押期间，整整有半年时间，其家人均无任何他们的消息，知道后也不许家里人接见、只叫存钱，不许带进物品，庭审也没有通知家属。最终，<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">苏坤刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，</b>王翠娥刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">苏明霞：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">河北省平山县城关镇中白楼村人，女，法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">1966</span>年生。<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月中共发动了对法轮大法的全面迫害，苏明霞女士多次被抓捕、关押，期间遭到恶警无故殴打、辱骂、虐待。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日，苏明霞在孟贤壁集市上讲法轮功时，被<span lang="EN-US">110</span>警察抓捕，被关押至石家庄第二看守所关押近<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年，期间不准家人探视。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月，苏明霞被石家庄正定县法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年半，关押到河北省女子监狱。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">宿慧娜：女，</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">辽宁省丹东市人，法轮功学员。在北京工作，居住在北京市昌平区沙河镇。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日，宿慧娜贴法轮功传单，被监控录像看到后，被跟踪抓捕到北京市朝阳分局大屯派出所。警察在她包里翻出法轮功粘贴，随后对她抄家。宿慧娜后被关押到北京市朝阳看守所。宿慧娜被抓捕、关押在北京市朝阳看守所<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年多，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月被北京朝阳区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">隋英华：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">辽宁省抚顺法轮功学员。男，一九七二年一月四日出生，清原县清原镇浑河街人，<span lang="EN-US">2000</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日依法去北京为法轮功上访，和几十个法轮功学员在北京的天安门广场打开一条长<span lang="EN-US">99</span>米的巨型横幅，被抓捕，<span lang="EN-US">2001</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月被北京东城区法院被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年半。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日，隋英华在工作中，被山西省太原市古交派出所五个警察和辽宁省抚顺市清原县河南（腰站）派出所警察抓捕，并抄家，刑事拘留，关押在清原县看守所。后辽宁省抚顺望花区法院法官执法犯法，判清原县法轮功学员隋英华<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">隋永彦</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">：<span lang="EN-US">1950</span>年代生人，辽宁丹东法轮功学员，原建筑造价工程师。面对中共对法轮功迫害，隋永彦曾经<span lang="EN-US">3</span>次被丹东站前派出所警察抓捕、抄家，并被劳教、判刑。<span lang="EN-US">2000</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月，隋永彦遭抓捕、抄家后，被关进辽宁本溪教养院，遭劳教<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。<span lang="EN-US">2004</span>年，警察到隋永彦的工作单位实施抓捕，他工作用的电脑也被抄走，并被抄家。<span lang="EN-US">2004</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日，隋永彦被关押在盘锦监狱迫害<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月，隋永彦又被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，被劫入本溪监狱迫害。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日上午遭丹东市振安区珍珠路派出所警察监控、抓捕、构陷，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月末被判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">索南次帕（藏）</span></b><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">西藏昌都地区八宿县人，青年作家，曾在定日县经商。曾因持有达赖喇嘛尊者法像而两次入狱。<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年，索南次帕就曾被冠上“危害国家安全罪”而被判两年徒刑；<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月，他再次被当局指控“撰写煽动民族矛盾文章、散发达赖喇嘛法像、破坏社会稳定”等，在拉萨遭关押一个月左右，并被处以罚款。索南次帕于<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19&nbsp;</span>日在西藏首都拉萨再次遭当地公安拘捕，这是<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年以来第三次遭到中共公安的拘捕。目前亲友仍不清楚索南次帕被捕的原因，以及关押地点等情况。后音信全无。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">索南达夫（藏）：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">出生年月不详，四川省甘孜藏族自治州炉霍县人，藏族，中国在押政治犯。因中共当局在西藏及其周边各省涉藏地区强硬推行“爱国和法制宣传教育”活动，不准挂达赖喇嘛头像等，引发多地藏民强烈不满；<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月，四川省甘孜州炉霍县僧俗藏人亦举行大规模和平示威游行，要求西藏自由，信仰自由，并高呼达赖喇嘛万岁等口号，随即遭到中共警方的武力镇压和大规模抓捕，警民冲突升级；最终导致多人被打死打伤，上百藏人在当时及随后被抓或失踪，数十人被当局判处<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>个月至无期徒刑不等的刑期；索南达夫本人也因积极参与抗议示威活动，被警方以“聚众闹事”、 “参与炉霍县抗议示威和严重影响公共秩序的非法聚集”以及与境外势力有染等为由抓走，后被甘孜藏族自治州炉霍县法院以同罪由重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年。目前服刑地点不详。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">索南公保（藏）：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">1985</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">年出生，四川省甘孜藏族自治州新吧龙县人，藏名<span lang="EN-US">Solnam Gonpo</span>，原甘孜藏族自治州新龙县塘吉乡（音译）小学厨师，藏族人权捍卫者。曾因积极参与罢耕运动和抵制中共控制的藏历新年庆祝活动，<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，被当局怀疑参与在该县塘吉乡（音译）境内的一起有关抗议中共暴政，散发传单、呼吁西藏独立的示威活动；事发当天因该抗议活动引发警民冲突，乡政府办公大楼发生火灾，<span lang="EN-US"> 2009</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日，随于被新龙县警方强行抓捕，并被以涉嫌“煽动分裂国家罪”和“扰乱社会秩序罪”刑事拘留，关押于四川省成都市某看守所；<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，被四川省甘孜州中级法院以“煽动分裂国家”和“扰乱社会秩序”两项罪名判处无期徒刑。目前在四川省德阳市黄许镇德阳监狱服刑。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">索南林珠（藏）：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">四川甘孜藏区炉霍县人，藏族人权捍卫者。<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日，在西藏康区炉霍县境内发生大规模和平示威活动后，中共军警釆取武力镇压，导致云丹为首的多名藏人被开枪打死或打伤，上百人遭捕。<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日中共当局对<span lang="EN-US">16</span>名遭捕的藏人进行判决，其中一名藏人被判终身监禁，另有多人遭<span lang="EN-US">1</span>至<span lang="EN-US">13</span>年不等的有期徒刑。这<span lang="EN-US">16</span>名被判藏人中，已确切得知的有<span lang="EN-US">10</span>名藏人具体情况，其中：索南林珠，<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">30</span>多岁，被判无期徒刑。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">孙策贞：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">山东青岛法轮功学员，<span lang="EN-US">1956</span>年生，家住青岛市城阳区流亭街道赵村小区。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月份，孙策贞在流亭李家女姑集上告诉百姓法轮大法好的真相时，被便衣绑架。后由家人「取保」回家。孙吉芬在家期间，不断有青岛市即墨区法院人员骚扰、传唤。青岛市即墨区法院要求其和家人及律师到法院开庭。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月份，孙策贞被即墨区法院人员抓捕，开庭。此后，孙策贞被关押至今。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月得知，孙策贞老人被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">孙大午：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1954</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月生，河北省徐水县高林村镇郎五庄村人，河北大午农牧集团有限公司董事长。 孙大午初中毕业后曾待过山西临汾二十八军八十二师与徐水县农行，这两个经历让他发现农牧业可以发展经营。<span lang="EN-US">1985</span>年他创立大午农牧集团有限公司，担任董事长，以一千只鸡与五十头猪起家。担任董事长期间，孙大午于<span lang="EN-US">1996</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月获颁河北省养鸡状元荣誉。<span lang="EN-US">1995</span>年，大午集团已经成为中国五百大私营企业之一，孙大午也获选为保定市人大代表。<span lang="EN-US">1996</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月，他当选保定市禽蛋产业联合会理事长。<span lang="EN-US">2001</span>年，孙大午除了大午集团董事长外，亦兼任大午学校校长；<span lang="EN-US">2002</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月，他被中国农业大学农民问题研究所聘请为高级研究员。<span lang="EN-US"> 2003</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日，徐水县公安局通知大午网站：该网站发表的《小康社会的建设及难点》《悼念李慎之》《两位民间商人关于中国的时局及历史的对话》三篇文章严重损害了国家机关的形象，整顿网站，停止营业<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，罚款<span lang="EN-US">15000</span>元。<span lang="EN-US"> 2003</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日，他被指向三千多户农民借款达一亿八千多万元而被捕，并以非法集资的罪名遭到收押，并被指控其非法持有弹药；两位弟弟大午集团副董事长孙志华、总经理孙德华和集团的财务处长也都被扣留。 最终徐水县法院以非法吸收公众存款的罪名判其有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年、缓刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，罚金<span lang="EN-US">10</span>万元，大午集团同时也被判处罚金三十万元。于<span lang="EN-US">2003</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日出狱回家。孙大午于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日被河北高碑店市公安局刑事拘留，指控他涉嫌寻衅滋事罪和破坏生产经营。同时，其妻子、两个儿子儿媳、公司高管等<span lang="EN-US">28</span>人一并被抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，河北大午集团此前被“指定居所监视居住”的<span lang="EN-US">7</span>位当事人家属，分别收到公安送达的逮捕通知书。孙大午被控<span lang="EN-US">8</span>项罪名，分别是：非法吸收公众存款罪、寻衅滋事罪、非法采矿罪、聚众冲击国家机关罪、非法占用农用地罪、强迫交易罪、破坏生产经营罪、妨害公务罪。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日<span lang="EN-US">9</span>时至<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日<span lang="EN-US">16</span>时，大午案经历<span lang="EN-US">14</span>天庭审后当庭宣判：大午农牧集团有限公司：罚金<span lang="EN-US">3050</span>万元，依法追缴违法所得<span lang="EN-US">1447.54</span>万元，责令大午农牧集团有限公司退赔非法集资款项人民币<span lang="EN-US">10.37</span>亿元。孙大午被判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">18</span>年，并处罚金<span lang="EN-US">311</span>万元；刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2038</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">孙德华：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">大午集团副监事长，孙大午二弟。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日凌晨，河北大午农牧集团负责人孙大午及其亲属并集团子公司法人等近<span lang="EN-US">30</span>人被警方突击抓捕。其后，包括孙大午妻子刘会茹等部分公司高管，被以“非法吸收公众存款”罪名批捕，而孙大午等其他公司高管以“指定居所监视居住”的方式被采取强制措施。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，河北大午集团此前被“指定居所监视居住”的<span lang="EN-US">7</span>位当事人家属，分别收到公安送达的逮捕通知书。孙德华被控罪名：非法吸收公众存款罪、寻衅滋事罪、非法采矿罪、聚众冲击国家机关罪、非法占用农用地罪、强迫交易罪、破坏生产经营罪、妨害公务罪。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日<span lang="EN-US">9</span>时至<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日<span lang="EN-US">16</span>时，大午案经历<span lang="EN-US">14</span>天庭审后当庭宣判：孙德华被判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">12</span>年，并处罚金<span lang="EN-US">190</span>万元；刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2032</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">孙德香：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">女，<span lang="EN-US">1956</span>年生，黑龙江省伊春市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，中共开始疯狂迫害法轮功，孙德香遭中共邪党人员抓捕、关押，<span lang="EN-US">2010</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日曾经被判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月初，孙德香被伊春市公安局恶警秘密抓捕。孙德香后被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，现已被劫入黑龙江省女子监狱。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月初。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">孙广利：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">黑龙江省齐齐哈尔市法轮功学员。孙广利、孟素英夫妇，黑龙江省齐齐哈尔市碾子山区人，暂住辽宁省沈阳市。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日晚<span lang="EN-US">7</span>点多孙广利、孟素英夫妇，在沈阳市辽中区<span lang="EN-US">6</span>间房镇的<span lang="EN-US">1</span>个村子里发了几张告诉世人如何躲避瘟疫的方法，被人诬告，<span lang="EN-US">6</span>间房派出所的警察将<span lang="EN-US">2</span>人抓捕到当地派出所进行关押。 由于那时中国疫情严重，看守所不接收，次日晚<span lang="EN-US">7</span>点多将<span lang="EN-US">2</span>人放回家中。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日晚<span lang="EN-US">7</span>点左右，东街派出所的<span lang="EN-US">5</span>、<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个警察又到家中将夫妻<span lang="EN-US">2</span>人强行抓捕到东街派出所。<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日晚，丈夫孙广利被关押到沈阳第二看守所，妻子孟素英被关押到沈阳第一看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日傍晚，他们的家人接到法院通知：孙广利、孟素英夫妇判决已下来，最终两人均被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">孙桂昌：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">吉林省德惠市五台乡法轮功学员。孙桂昌和肖永芬夫妇各被非法判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年，已经于<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月份被羁押到公主岭监狱和吉林省女子监狱。孙桂昌和妻子肖永芬<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日被不法警察入室绑架。孙贵昌被送到德惠市拘留所非法拘留五天。肖永芬被送到长春第二看守所检查身体，不合格拒收，第二天下午<span lang="EN-US">7</span>点多钟放回家，被监视居住。后来，孙桂昌被非法关押德惠看守所。肖永芬因身体和精神状况被放回家，并被监视居住。<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日左右，吉林省公安厅数个警察将在其女儿看家的肖永芬绑架。据悉，肖永芬以前在长春黑嘴子劳教所被迫害得精神失常，现在患有高血压和糖尿病（后期），脚部严重溃烂，现在被关押在吉林省女子监狱八监区；孙桂昌被关押在公主岭监狱九监区。多年来，上述两个监狱公开执法犯法，利用死人床、坐小板凳、长期剥夺睡眠、电棍电击、殴打、上绳等各种酷刑残害和转化善良无辜的法轮功学员，多人被迫害致伤、致残、致疯、致死。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">孙桂芳：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">大连市金州区法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">1952</span>生。因修炼法轮功，<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年曾经被劳教<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年、在马三家劳动教养院遭受迫害。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，大连市公安局金州分局国保和金州区拥政派出所，由金州区古城甲区社区主任王新配合诱骗说楼下漏水，闯入家中绑架孙桂芳和另两位法轮功学员，并非法抄家，抢走法轮功书籍若干以及大量私人物品。孙桂芳<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日被送大连市看守所关押，同年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日被批捕。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日，孙桂芳老人在大连市金州区法院被庭审，律师在法庭上为孙桂芳做了无罪辩护。后得知孙桂芳被大连市金州区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">孙继萍</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">：辽宁锦州凌海市法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">68</span>岁。在中共对法轮功的迫害中，孙继萍与丈夫周永林被中共绑架、关押，劳教，在派出所、看守所、劳教所遭酷刑折磨。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，孙继萍与丈夫周永林在盘锦市锦采新区大集上告诉人们“法轮大法好”时，被凌海市公安局闫家镇派出所警察绑架，被隔离二十一天后（<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日），孙继萍被非法关押到锦州市女子看守所，周永林被非法关押到凌海市看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月，凌海市法院对孙继萍与丈夫周永林每人各判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年、罚金各一万元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">孙建锋</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">：宁夏中卫市中宁县法轮功学员。自<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年中共对法轮功持续至今已逾二十多年的迫害中，<span lang="EN-US">1972</span>年生的孙建锋先生曾经被劳教<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年半、判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日晚，孙建锋先生被一小区的保安诬告，警察将孙建锋绑架后搜身，并闯入孙建锋家抄家，劫掠了两本大法书籍，随后将孙建锋劫持到中宁县看守所关押，后孙建锋被批捕。孙建锋先生<span lang="EN-US">2010</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日被判<span lang="EN-US">6</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>个月。孙建锋已经被关押到宁夏石嘴山监狱服刑。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">孙江怡：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">湖北荆州法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日下午<span lang="EN-US">5</span>点多钟，丈夫李行军从母亲家出来，刚下楼，就被国保、西门派出所警察、学校保卫科等多人抓捕，他们对他拳打脚踢，打的满脸是血。被强行带上警车后，就送到西门看守所去了。妻子孙江怡也被抓走。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日才开庭。李行军、孙江怡夫妇被庭审，两人都被判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">孙俊：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">大连市中山区人，大连市热电公司职工，法轮功学员，良心犯。孙俊因是张霞的丈夫，<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日下班后发现家被抄，就到青云小学询问，才知妻子已被民主广场派出所警方抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，孙俊到民主广场派出所询问妻子情况时也被警方扣押，后送姚家看守所羁押。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日，夫妇二人被中山区检察院以涉嫌“邪教罪”正式批捕，后被秘密开庭，最终被大连市中山区法院一审以“利用邪教组织破坏法律实施罪”判处<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>个月。其不服提起上诉，大连市中级法院未经二审开庭即对他维持原判。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月底，孙俊被送往大连市监狱服刑。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">孙利：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">河北省唐山市法轮功学员，男，原唐山钢铁公司职工。因修炼法轮功，曾被劳教、判刑迫害。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日，河北唐山市东窑派出所警察，在一位老年法轮功学员家，抓捕了孙利。孙利被关押在唐山市第一看守所 。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日在路北区法院被庭审，后被判刑<span lang="EN-US">9</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2029</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">孙萌：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">孙大午大儿子、集团董事长。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日凌晨，河北大午农牧集团负责人孙大午及其亲属并集团子公司法人等近<span lang="EN-US">30</span>人被警方突击抓捕。其后，包括孙大午妻子刘会茹等部分公司高管，被以“非法吸收公众存款”罪名批捕，而孙大午等其他公司高管以“指定居所监视居住”的方式被采取强制措施。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，河北大午集团此前被“指定居所监视居住”的<span lang="EN-US">7</span>位当事人家属，分别收到公安送达的逮捕通知书。孙萌被控罪名：非法吸收公众存款罪、非法占用农用地罪、非法采矿罪、强迫交易罪、诈骗罪。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日<span lang="EN-US">9</span>时至<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日<span lang="EN-US">16</span>时，大午案经历<span lang="EN-US">14</span>天庭审后当庭宣判：孙萌被判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">12</span>年，并处罚金<span lang="EN-US">190</span>万元；刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2032</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">孙润桃：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">河北省张家口市沽源县法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日下午，沽源县法轮功学员高清秀、孙润桃、赵梅在长梁乡顺路讲法轮功、免费传递法轮功法轮功资料时，遭人恶告，遭警方抓捕。孙润桃和高清秀<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日，分别被张北县法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年和<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，勒索罚款<span lang="EN-US">2</span>万元。孙润桃刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">孙茜：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">加拿大华裔女富商。孙茜是北京利德曼生物化学公司的创始人，<span lang="EN-US">2007</span>年获加拿大国籍，<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年和<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年登上胡润中国富豪榜，身家<span lang="EN-US">35</span>亿。由于操劳过度，身体严重透支，孙茜患上多种疾病，多方医治无效。在<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年她学习炼法轮功。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，孙茜正在家中与表妹聊天，警方突然闯入抄家，搜出法轮功相关书籍后，将她抓捕。期间，孙茜多次遭受酷刑，被铐在铁椅子上，被辣椒水喷脸。全天被戴上镣铐，强制洗脑，强迫放弃她的信仰。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日，孙茜一案在北京朝阳法院温榆河法庭开庭，孙茜获刑<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;">孙士伟：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1953</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年生，黑龙江穆棱市教师进修学校美术教研员，法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2005</span>年，孙士伟因在一次歌会上为了表达对大法师父的敬仰，唱了一首大法弟子创作的歌曲，被人举报，九月二十三日被警察突然闯入家中绑架，遭毒打折磨，<span lang="EN-US">2006</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月被判刑八年，在佳木斯莲江口监狱遭受了种种迫害。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日下午，穆棱市建行小区的一位老人曹淑芳家中的玻璃碎了，孙士伟、高朋光、高永丽三人帮其修理。国保警察突然出现抓捕了孙士伟、高朋光、高永丽三人，并抄了三人的家。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，海林市法院下判决，高永丽被诬判<span lang="EN-US">6</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>个月，高朋光和孙士伟被诬判<span lang="EN-US">6</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，分别处以两万罚金。孙士伟刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt;">孙永勤：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt;">男，<span lang="EN-US">1966</span>年生，家住东港市。<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日晚<span lang="EN-US">9</span>点多钟，孙永勤在开车回家的路上，被便衣警察劫持，车和钥匙被抢。十点左右，妻子张小平正坐在客厅沙发上看书。十多个便衣警察拿着抢到的门钥匙破门而入，将张小平和她女儿铐住，当时张小平的女儿已经睡下，恶警在被窝里将她抓捕。恶警疯狂抄家，抢走法轮大法书籍、真相资料若干、现金十万余元（家中生活费及生意周转资金，还有她女儿的工资<span lang="EN-US">6</span>千元均被洗劫一空）、手机、存折、银行卡、打印机<span lang="EN-US">3</span>台、电脑两台。<span lang="EN-US">1</span>家<span lang="EN-US">3</span>口全被恶警非法抓捕到东港市开发区公安所审讯。孙永勤、张小平被非法关押进东港看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，东港市法院对孙永勤重判<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年，现被非法关押在沈阳第<span lang="EN-US">1</span>监狱<span lang="EN-US">2</span>监区<span lang="EN-US">2</span>小队。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><a name="_Hlk52322719"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">孙永耀：</span></b></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk52322719;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1970</span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk52322719;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日出生，安徽省阜南县人，阜南县鹿城镇刘寨村孙西组<span lang="EN-US">13</span>号公民，基督徒，安徽省阜南县基督教堂主任牧师，中国在押良心犯。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月，其所在教会接到当地政府发来的要求拆除教堂通知，称其教堂因地处政府要进行街道棚改项目改造规划的范畴，故而必须拆除；由于地方当局仅对其所在教会提出单方面拆迁补偿方案，并称如要教堂异地重建，政府将不给予相应补偿；因此通告方案明显有失公允，立刻遭到其及教会众信徒的坚决反对，遂遭地方当局的恶意报复与打击；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日，正当众信徒在教会举行聚会和敬拜时，突然被官方拆迁公司闯入，并在无任何合法档及拆除手续的情况下实施强拆，因事发突然，教会里面的所有物品均未及时搬出，终致所有财物几近损毁；因其坚决反对政府强拆教堂的举动，同年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日，遂与教会主任耿宜敏等神职人员一同被阜南市警方抓捕，次日被以涉“聚众扰乱社会秩序罪”刑拘；<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk52322719;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">同年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，被阜阳县检察院予以批捕；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日，其案在安徽省阜南县法院开庭受审；<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日，被该法院一审以“聚众扰乱社会秩序罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月；其不服，提起上诉；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，安徽省阜阳市中级法院经二审裁决，认为“原判认定的部分事实不清，证据不足”，故撤销原判，发回重审。目前被羁押于阜南县看守所。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></p> <span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk52322719;"></span> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">孙占国：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">吉林省松原市干安县法轮功学员。家住松原市干安县唱子村，在中共对法轮功的疯狂迫害中，孙占国曾连续两次被非法劳教，曾被关押在吉林省九台饮马河劳教所，遭受酷刑虐待。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月被干安县油田采油厂派出所抓捕，被关押一年后，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月被干安县法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">孙志芬</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">：山西太原市老年法轮功学员。太原市公安局迎泽分局警察<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日非法闯民宅，抄家抓捕法轮功学员孙志芬（<span lang="EN-US">60</span>岁）、王素平（<span lang="EN-US">67</span>岁）、罗保军（<span lang="EN-US">62</span>岁）、张清香（<span lang="EN-US">69</span>岁）、张润英（<span lang="EN-US">71</span>岁）、郭润鲜（<span lang="EN-US">68</span>岁）、田玉琴（<span lang="EN-US">60</span>岁）、胡兰英（<span lang="EN-US">65</span>岁），其中多数是老太太。山西省太原市这八位老年法轮功学员被非法关押近一年后得知被迎泽区法院非法判刑、勒索罚款，并被劫持到监狱。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">被判刑<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年，罚金<span lang="EN-US">3</span>万元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2028</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">孙志华：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">大午集团副监事长，孙大午亲属。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日凌晨，河北大午农牧集团负责人孙大午及其亲属并集团子公司法人等近<span lang="EN-US">30</span>人被警方突击抓捕。其后，包括孙大午妻子刘会茹等部分公司高管，被以“非法吸收公众存款”罪名批捕，而孙大午等其他公司高管以“指定居所监视居住”的方式被采取强制措施。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，河北大午集团此前被“指定居所监视居住”的<span lang="EN-US">7</span>位当事人家属，分别收到公安送达的逮捕通知书。孙志华被控罪名：寻衅滋事罪、非法采矿罪、聚众冲击国家机关罪、非法占用农用地罪、破坏生产经营罪、妨害公务罪。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日<span lang="EN-US">9</span>时至<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日<span lang="EN-US">16</span>时，大午案经历<span lang="EN-US">14</span>天庭审后当庭宣判：孙志华被判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">9</span>年，并处罚金<span lang="EN-US">55</span>万元；刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2029</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">孙治军：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1963</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年出生，河南省郑州市中原区人，郑州市中原区西流湖街道孙庄北苑村民，维权访民，村民选举参选人，公义维权举报人，人权捍卫者，中国在押维权人士。<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月，曾因所在河南省郑州市中原区西流湖区孙庄村被政府强制拆迁，且其及另五名住户所获拆迁补偿与政府承诺拆迁标准严重不符（即未按补偿标准少给各家一块宅基地），随被迫连手走上信访之路；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日，因此前多次信访维权了无果效，就于中共五中全会前夕，其等六人一起前往北京做进一步信访投诉，随遭郑州当局的严厉打压；很快，其被郑州当局截访人员强行遣返，并于<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日被郑州市中原分局警方以“寻衅滋事”为罪由处行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">14</span>天；同年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日，因其不服此行政处罚之决定，故将郑州市中原区分局告上郑州市铁路运输法庭；<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，因其又将郑州市中原区西流湖办事处书记胡志军、中原区西流湖办事处孙庄包村书记艾超，以及中原区西流湖办事处原孙庄村村委会主任孙耀东等政府官员实名举报，称此三人具有滥用职权、动用警械、垄断村资源、伪造宅基证骗取宅基院补偿的安置房和违规套取国家迁拆补偿款等违纪违法行为，遂立遭管理者当局的打击报复；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日，先被中原分局西流湖派出所警方以涉嫌“妨害社会管理秩序罪”传唤带走，随后又被中原区警方以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”转刑事拘留；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日，被郑州市中原区检察院以同罪由予以批捕；据悉，其在看守所内遭到严重人权伤害，经常被强制要求站立<span lang="EN-US">1</span>小时，既不能蹲下，也不能坐着，导致曾多次晕倒被急救。目前被羁押于郑州市第三看守所。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">孙忠琴：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">女，<span lang="EN-US">1952</span>年生，辽宁凤城法轮功学员。孙忠琴因为向民众讲清法轮功，<span lang="EN-US">2007</span>年，曾被马三家劳教所劳教<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年，期间受尽酷刑和奴役，<span lang="EN-US">2011</span>年被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，在辽宁女子监狱，被恶警指使犯人关进小黑屋里暴力殴打、扒光衣服浇凉水等。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，丹东市凤城市法轮功学员鞠世淼、孙忠琴、佟秀红，在凤城大兴镇，给村民送明慧新年台历、福字和期刊等，被大兴镇政法综治委员宋传刚等人抓捕，后被构陷到丹东市振安区法院。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日，<span lang="EN-US">3</span>位法轮功学员被丹东市振安区法院判刑：鞠世淼被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，勒索罚款<span lang="EN-US">5</span>千元；孙忠琴<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，勒索罚款<span lang="EN-US">5</span>千元；佟秀红<span lang="EN-US">11</span>个月，勒索罚款<span lang="EN-US">3</span>千元。佟秀红于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日被“取保候审”，已回家。孙忠琴刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">孙转建：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">河南商丘法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，孙转建被抓捕，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>号开庭。被判<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年有期徒刑。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>号，被关押到河南郑州监狱服刑。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/10/23/%E4%BA%8C%E9%9B%B6%E4%BA%8C%E4%B8%80%E5%B9%B4%E5%8D%81%E6%9C%88%E4%BA%8C%E5%8D%81%E4%B8%89%E6%97%A5%E5%A4%A7%E9%99%86%E7%BB%BC%E5%90%88%E6%B6%88%E6%81%AF-432812.html#211022211210-2"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/10/23/%E4%BA%8C%E9%9B%B6%E4%BA%8C%E4%B8%80%E5%B9%B4%E5%8D%81%E6%9C%88%E4%BA%8C%E5%8D%81%E4%B8%89%E6%97%A5%E5%A4%A7%E9%99%86%E7%BB%BC%E5%90%88%E6%B6%88%E6%81%AF-432812.html#211022211210-2</span></b></a></span><b
